UK Reorganizing National Defense; Cabinet Considering Establishing Committee 19

London—The cabinet met today and has drafted a £300 million rearmament plan. The National Defense Subcommittee has already held twelve meetings this month, and today's cabinet meeting approved the plan. The needs of British national defense were reportedly discussed at the cabinet meeting, including: 1) allocating the funds to cover the expenses of various national defense departments over the next three years; 2) methods of raising funds, whether through the issuance of treasury bills or public bonds; 3) adjusting the plan for Imperial defense. In the future, a committee may be formed, consisting of Minister without Portfolio Sir Thomas Inskip together with personnel from the general staff of the army, navy, and air force; 4) proposing to re-establish a munitions department or other agency to prepare for industrial mobilization; 5) issuing a white paper in mid-March explaining the reasons for Britain's rearmament. (National Telegram, 17th)

London—The Cabinet held a meeting today and reportedly considered establishing two committees, both named the National Defense Coordination Committee, one responsible for national defense matters within the UK and the other responsible for the defense of overseas dominions and territories. This plan to reorganize national defense was proposed by the Cabinet's National Defense Committee and has been thoroughly discussed by the Cabinet. It is reported that it will take four or five years to complete. However, the government, recognizing the need for a great effort in the industrial sector for rearmament, does not want to delay the process for too long and will try to shorten the deadline as much as possible. It is generally believed that the capacity of British aircraft factories should also be expanded to build the necessary aircraft in accordance with the government's air force plan. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

London—The Times recently reported that the government's rearmament plan requires funding of £230,000,000. The white paper on this plan will be published in early March, and the House of Commons will submit it for discussion on the 9th of next month. To alleviate unemployment, the government will allocate most of the work of the rearmament plan to regions with the highest unemployment rates. In addition, the government will solemnly declare that it will make every effort to improve the diplomatic situation, and once the international tension eases, it will gradually implement this plan. US Supreme Court Decision: Tennessee Valley Authority Act Does Not Violate the Constitution 24

Washington – The Supreme Court today ruled that the Tennessee Valley Authority project is constitutional, and that the measures taken by the Tennessee Valley Authority, created under the act, are also valid. This is a major victory for the government, which had previously suffered setbacks in its political and economical plans with the Supreme Court's decisions against the National Industrial Recovery Act and the Agricultural Adjustment Act. The court ruled that the government has the right to sell electricity from the Wilson Dam and expressed full support for selling electricity elsewhere in the river basin in the future. Only one of the nine judges dissented. Chief Justice Hughes read the judgment, stating that the federal government, under the constitution, has the right to: construct sluice gates at the Wilson Dam to facilitate navigation; sell electricity generated by these sluice gates; and lay electrical cables to transport electricity to a "substantial market." This ruling clearly permits the federal government to construct similar hydroelectric dams on other rivers, but it does not clarify whether the government has the right to invest in laying electrical lines in rural or urban areas, as this issue was not mentioned in the appeal. However, the government does have such plans. The appellant in this case was a preferred shareholder of the Alabama Power Company, which had previously monopolized the electrical business in Alabama. The Tennessee Valley Authority loaned money to electrical companies in various towns, allowing them to set up their own lines. The company's common stockholders then sold the company's electrical lines to the Authority. At that time, the preferred shareholders came forward to object. After litigation, the current judgment was reached. However, there may still be disputes regarding other issues related to the Tennessee Valley Authority Act in the future. (National Telegram, 17th)

Washington – The Senate today passed the independent agencies budget bill, which includes $1,730,000,000 for redeeming veterans' bonus bonds and $440,000,000 for agricultural relief. However, it did not specify methods for raising funds. The bill has now been sent back to the House for agreement on amendments. (National Telegram, 17th)

Main Battleship Tonnage Issue: France Convenes Meeting; Content Strictly Confidential 25

Paris – The chief French representative to the naval conference, Ambassador to the UK Corbin, recently returned to France to report to the government on the situation at the conference, especially regarding the issue of battleship tonnage. Naval Minister Piétri has convened a special meeting to discuss the matter. In addition to Corbin, those attending the meeting include Naval Chief of Staff Vice Admiral Darlan, naval conference representative Colonel Trousseau, and Assistant Director of the Political Affairs Department of the Foreign Ministry, Massigli. Government officials believe that the details of the meeting should not be disclosed at this time, and have declined to issue a statement. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

London – The chief French representative to the naval conference, Corbin, and the Italian representative, Rear Admiral Piaccia, recently returned to their respective countries to report to their governments on the situation at the conference. According to sources here, Corbin and Piaccia submitted a compromise proposal from the UK regarding the issue of battleship tonnage to their respective governments for review. The proposal suggests allowing the UK and the US to temporarily build a certain number of 35,000-ton battleships, with the tonnage to be reduced later. Conference officials believe that this proposal will be acceptable to France and Italy. In addition to the compromise proposal mentioned above, Corbin and Piaccia also submitted a draft protocol to their governments for review. This protocol addresses the issue of exchanging information between naval powers after the establishment of a future naval agreement. It also proposes that the signatory countries authorize the UK to submit the future agreement to other countries, so that those countries can sign and participate, or offer suggestions and consult with the UK on modifications. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

London – According to sources at the naval conference, the conference will announce a postponement within a few days. British naval experts believe that if the conference fails to establish a qualitative limitation agreement and immediately announces a postponement, the policies adopted by the various naval powers will depend on the shipbuilding programs of Germany and Japan. Japan's shipbuilding plans generally fall into one of the following two categories: building only extremely fast cruisers, equipped with the best military equipment and the strongest armor, so that in the event of war, when a foreign battle fleet with lower speed arrives in the Pacific, these cruisers can be used to cut off their rear lines; or building super battleships with a displacement of over 45,000 tons. If the latter occurs, the United States will not be willing to show weakness and will also build similar large ships. However, these types of warships would have difficulty passing through the Panama Canal. If Japan takes the second path, the United States may allocate huge sums to modify the canal, or use these large ships exclusively by the Pacific Fleet and not include them in the Atlantic Fleet. If that were to happen, the entire US naval strategy would be completely changed. As for Germany, if it also builds large warships, the Kiel Canal would be in the same position as the Panama Canal. However, the German fleet can still sail into the North Sea through the straits of the Baltic Sea, which is different from the US fleet. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

French Treasury Borrows from Britain to Establish Fund: Huge Sum of 40 Million Pounds; Largest International Loan Since 1931; British and French Banks Agree on Measures to Protect Exchange Rates 29

London – According to news today, Britain has agreed to lend 40 million pounds to the French Treasury. This is the largest international loan involving Britain since 1931. Several British banks are acting as lenders, while the British government and the Bank of England have no direct involvement. However, the Bank of France and the Bank of England have agreed on measures to protect foreign exchange rates from fluctuations. Since the British Exchange Equalisation Account is confirmed to not be involved in the loan transfer, Londoners are unaware of the nature of the measures taken to transfer such a large amount of foreign exchange without disturbing market equilibrium. In the event that the loan has not been fully repaid and France has abandoned the gold standard, how will British bankers be protected from exchange rate losses? This guarantee issue is currently highly confidential, and outsiders have no way of knowing the details. However, considering the low interest rate on this loan, it can be inferred that it is attached to guarantee conditions. (Reuters, 18th)

Paris – Negotiations between the French Treasury and a British banking syndicate regarding a loan to the French Treasury were successfully concluded in London this afternoon. The total amount of the loan is 40 million pounds, with an annual interest rate of 3%, and a term of nine months. A spokesperson for the Ministry of Finance issued a statement explaining the nature of the loan, stating that France does not need to issue treasury bills in London. The British Rothschild Brothers Bank will simply make 40 million pounds available for France's use. After every three months, France can repay part or all of the loan early. This type of loan is a common practice. The French Treasury has previously sought assistance from the British market, which is no different from the recent need for French capital to assist the British market. Looking back to mid-1935, more than 16,000,000,000 French francs flowed out of France, which inevitably affected the financial market, leading to tightening. In addition, the revenue from various direct taxes is low in the first six months of each year, and the need for funds is urgent, making it necessary to negotiate a short-term loan. Once the tax revenue is abundant in the second half of the year, the loan can be repaid, and so on. Financial figures also said that the annual interest rate of 3% for the loan can be considered low. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

Records of a trip to the Desert (6) 77

— Jin Dui

8. The Manufacturing Process of Gansu Tobacco

Tobacco is a major product of Gansu, divided into four types: cotton tobacco, strip tobacco (i.e., green tobacco), yellow tobacco, and hemp strip tobacco. Although there are four main types of tobacco, the manufacturing methods are generally the same. However, in the selection of raw materials, each type is chosen for its suitability for a particular tobacco color and a specific dye is prepared to enhance its appearance. The selection of raw materials and the preparation process involve some trouble, as shown in the following procedures:

Step 1: Removing the Stems (commonly called "tearing the tobacco"). The branches and leaf veins of the tobacco leaves are completely removed by hand, leaving only the leaf blade. This work is mostly done by hired women and children. Wages are paid based on the amount of stems removed, about three or four copper coins per pound.

Step 2: Selecting the Leaves (commonly called "sorting the leaves"). Leaves with blemishes and wilted or yellowed parts are picked out, and the leaves are graded according to their quality. Leaves with green color and thick texture are considered superior; those that are not well-selected are of the next grade; and those with dark color and mildew are of the lowest grade. When selecting, if the weather is clear and the tobacco leaves are dry, some boiled water must be sprayed on them to soften the leaves before they are turned, so as not to break them too much.

Step 3: Blending Flavors Tobacco of the same variety has different flavors due to various factors such as climate, artificial fertilizers, and growing techniques. For example, Danshui tobacco has a light and fragrant taste; Xianshui tobacco has a plain and bland taste; Shudi tobacco has a sweet and mild taste; and Saidi tobacco has a strong and pungent taste. When collecting and transporting, they must be kept separate for temporary blending. (Spicy flavors are blended with sweet flavors, and bland flavors are blended with strong flavors.) Different workshops use different blends, resulting in different qualities of tobacco shreds. This skill depends entirely on the experience of the craftsmen, resulting in different outcomes.

Step 4: Preparing Colors Except for hemp strip tobacco, which is its natural color and does not require this procedure, green tobacco uses about two dou of gypsum powder, one jin and fourteen liang of purple flower, seven jin of sophora flower, one jin of alum, and one and a half jin of rock salt for every 450 jin of tobacco leaves. For cotton tobacco and yellow tobacco, the purple flower and sophora flower are reduced, and 30 jin of white salt, three and a half jin of turmeric, and three jin of scarlet are added. The above-listed pigments are first made into powder for color mixing.

Soup Method: Take a large wok, fill it with clear water, and first pour in the sophora flower, then heat it over a fire. Place a large urn next to it, which should be able to hold the total volume of water without overflowing. When the water in the wok has boiled three or four times, slowly pour the sophora flower water into the urn with a small wooden bucket or large ladle. At the same time, put the purple flower into the urn as you pour, stirring vigorously with a wooden stick. After all the purple flower has been added, add the alum and rock salt, continuing to stir. At this time, the water foams and boils, overflowing the urn. Put the previously prepared raw gypsum powder into a wooden frame, scoop water from the urn, pour it in while it is hot, and stir as you pour. The gypsum will turn into a green, sticky paste. The brightness and dullness of the color depend entirely on whether the mixture is appropriate. Knead the green paste into balls and place them on the roof or in an open area to dry in the sun. When they are half-dry, use a specially made upward-facing water board to crush them. After they are completely dry, grind them into a fine powder. Add a little sesame oil while grinding to make the color bright and not easily airborne. After grinding, sift it slowly with a fine bamboo sieve, resulting in an extremely fine powder, ready for use in the fifth step.

Step 5: Blending Colors Take the previously prepared tobacco leaves, first spray them with boiling water to soften them. Then take boiling sesame oil and spray it with a sprayer. Spray oil once for each layer of tobacco leaves that is sprinkled. After sieving the last layer, mix it evenly with a wooden rake and prepare for pressing.

Step 6: Pressing Place the already colored tobacco leaves in a rectangular wooden frame, about ten feet long and three to four feet wide. Place them in well, flatten them, cover them with a wooden board, and press them heavily with a specially made device for four to five hours. After pressing, cut them into three sections and stack them on top of each other. Place eight wooden beams underneath, two feet three inches long and three inches three minutes wide, and cover them with the same wooden beams. Tie them tightly with hemp rope to form a solid tobacco bundle.

Step 7: Shaving the Tobacco (commonly called "pushing the tobacco"). Place the previously pressed bundle upright, with two craftsmen per bundle. One person holds the scraper, and the other pulls from the front. The shaved shreds are collected by the person holding the scraper into a specially made small wooden box. The box is equipped with a live board and two axe-shaped wooden wedges. When the tobacco shreds are put in, the person pulling presses down, the live board tightens the wooden wedges, and the two ends are trimmed neatly and placed aside. The second batch of shaved shreds is collected into the second box. When the third batch of shavings falls, the first box can be opened and the finished tobacco blocks and tobacco bunches taken out. The tobacco shreds are then loaded in the same way as before, alternating in this way. The finished small squares are called tobacco bunches, and each bunch weighs two liang, four liang, or half a jin.

Step 8: Drying the Tobacco The newly made tobacco blocks still contain a small amount of moisture inside. If they are stacked layer upon layer, they are prone to mold and spoilage. Therefore, a bright and airy drying room must be set up in a spacious building, and shelves are installed for drying the tobacco. When the tobacco blocks are made, they are stacked on the shelves in a triangle shape, waiting to dry completely. Then they are collected and sold. Those that are shipped to other provinces are packed in boxes for transportation.

According to investigations, Gansu tobacco is sold as far as Tianjin, Beijing, Shanghai, and Wuhan; nearby provinces such as Shaanxi, Henan, Shandong, and Shanxi naturally have Gansu tobacco sold there. Pisi tobacco is a famous product of Fujian, but its sales area is not as wide as Gansu tobacco. However, according to people in the Gansu tobacco industry, "Before 1926, when tobacco prices were high, each jin sold for four qian two or three fen of silver or even four qian seven or eight fen (equivalent to six or seven jiao in foreign currency). However, since 1926, the value has gradually declined, day by day. In the past two or three years, the leaves have only sold for a few qian of silver per jin (around two jiao)." The reason for this is that in recent years, tobacco merchants across the country have reduced labor and materials, resulting in poor manufacturing or even the adulteration of fake materials. As a result, sales have suddenly decreased, and the pursuit of profit has turned into loss. This can be considered deserved. Furthermore, the popularity of domestic cigarettes, with their elaborate packaging and production, is far beyond the reach of Gansu tobacco. This is another reason for the decline of the Gansu tobacco industry. Therefore, to save it, it is necessary to cultivate superior tobacco leaves and explore exquisite manufacturing methods.

Fake Organization's Construction of a Highway Network Fake Railway Bureau Entrusts Mantetsu to Supervise Construction Spreads Throughout the Four Northeastern Provinces for Military Convenience 78

Shenyang Dispatch: After the Fake Railway Bureau was entrusted to be managed by Mantetsu by the fake organization, it immediately followed the orders of the Kwantung Army to carry out construction to facilitate military use. Under the guise of assisting railway operations, it operates long-distance buses, forcibly recruits laborers, and appropriates land to build highways to connect its railway lines. In the past three years, many highways have been built. The current bus routes operated by them are surveyed as follows:

(1) Within the Jurisdiction of the Fake Fengtian Railway Bureau: Andong Line, between Andong and Chengzitong; Fenghuang Line, between Fengcheng and Huangtupo; Fengfu Line, between Shenyang and Fushun; Hainiu Line, between Haicheng and Niuzhuang; Shenzheng Line, between Fanyang, Faku, and Kangping; Minzhang Line, between Xinmin and Zhangwu; Rehe Line, between Chaoyang and Beipiao, between Lingyuan and Chengde, between Yangchao and Lingyuan, between Chaoyang and Chifeng, between Pingquan and Chengde, between Chengde and Weichang, between Chengde and Fengning, between Chifeng and Weichang, between Weichang and Duolun.

(2) Within the Jurisdiction of the Fake Jilin Railway Bureau: Jingji Line, between Changchun and Jilin; Jingbei Line, between Changchun and Fuyu, between Houwafangzi and Nong'an, between Houwafangzi and Dalai; Dunhai Line, between Dunhua, Ning'an, Hailin, and Mudanjiang.

(3) Within the Jurisdiction of the Fake Qiqihar Railway Bureau: Jingtao Line, between Taonan and Dalai; Neihe Line, between Nehe and Nenjiang; Xingan Line, between Solun and Wenquan, between Hailar and Wenquan, between Taonan and Tuquan.

(4) Within the Jurisdiction of the Fake Harbin Railway Bureau: Dongman Line, between Dongning and Suifenhe, between Heihe and Aihun; Hatong Line, between Harbin, Jiamusi, Tongjiang, and Fujin.

Jianghan: Dike and Embankment Levy Labor for Repair - The Main Dike Along the River Determines Construction Methods - Hunan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces Share the Costs for the Construction of the Ma Hua Dike 79

Hankou Correspondence: Last summer, the prefectures of Hubei Province suffered severe flooding. Most of the dikes and embankments along the Jiang and Xiang Rivers collapsed, causing tens of millions of yuan in losses to rural communities. Many people were displaced, and the disaster was unprecedented in its severity. In addition to ordering the disaster relief agencies to do their best to provide relief and comfort to the victims, the provincial government has also formulated and distributed work-relief measures to repair the breaches. These measures include providing subsidies for construction and recruiting disaster victims for work-relief programs in order to prevent flooding in the coming year. However, the provincial government received an order from President Chiang, stating that "There are numerous dikes and embankments in Hubei Province, and many have been flooded or have collapsed. Considering the local situation, the Central Government has allocated funds for work-relief based on estimated budgets. It is imperative to quickly plan and start construction to repair the breaches and complete the work within a time limit to avoid further disasters." The Hubei Provincial Government also stated that the labor service season for water conservancy should be undertaken by the counties based on their local conditions. Orders were issued to this effect. Given the importance of water conservancy and transportation in Hubei Province, the Provincial Government has instructed the Water Disaster Relief Association to allocate work-relief funds based on the disaster situation in each county. Repairing the dikes should be specifically designated, and orders should be given for prompt action. With regard to the dike projects in each county, the main dikes should be repaired by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, as well as the Jingjiang Dike, the East Jinghe Dike, the Wuhui Dike, the Hanyang East Dike, and the Xinfeng and Hancheng Sanhuan embankments. All other civil dikes, civil embankments, and other water conservancy projects should be the responsibility of the county governments. They should follow the various plans and methods of national labor service, levy labor in a timely manner, select key areas for urgent work, and complete the projects on schedule. The original technical affairs instructors should be replaced by personnel dispatched by each county to receive segmented guidance and supervision from the responsible engineering offices. Tools should be self-provided by the people, and no subsidies will be given. After construction begins, the provincial government will send personnel to inspect the progress at any time. In addition to reporting to the headquarters for inspection and ordering the Department of Construction to instruct the Provincial Highway Engineering Office to act accordingly, special orders are issued to the commissioners of each district and the county magistrates of each county to comply. The estimated engineering, area, width, thickness, and cost of each dike are described below.

Zhang Gong Dike

The city of Hankou borders the Jiang and Xiang Rivers and is located in a low-lying area. Every flood season, it is surrounded by water on all sides. The northwest side is close to East Lake, and every year it relies on the Zhang Gong Dike for protection. The Zhang Gong Dike starts from the Boxue Academy in the west and ends at Dijiao in the northeast, serving as the only barrier for Hankou. There were originally no flood control dikes along the Yangtze River from Dijiao to Lower Taikoo. It relied on the Pinghan Railway embankment to protect against river water. After the great flood of 1931, a new dike was built along the river, and the dike surface was paved with crushed stone. From Lower Taikoo and beyond, up to Dakou Alley to Qiaokou along the Xiang River, it is still the old city area with streets and markets and numerous buildings. Except for raising the street level once, there have been no special risks in recent years. From Qiaokou to Shuitang, a small dike is built along the river to connect with the Zhang Gong Dike. This is the circular flood control embankment for the city of Hankou. After the great flood of 1931, the highest water level at the Jianghan Customs water gauge was 53.6 feet (equivalent to 28.40 meters on the Wusong datum). The entire city was submerged. In 1935, the Jiang and Xiang Rivers rose simultaneously and rapidly. From July 4th to July 14th, within ten days, the river water level rose sharply from 3.93 feet to 5.13 feet (27.65 meters). On the Zhang Gong Dike side, due to the rapid flow of the Xiang River, the water level reached 5.60 feet (29.04 meters), exceeding the great flood water level of 1931 by 2.4 feet. Therefore, the situation was particularly critical. Although rescue efforts were made, no major disaster occurred, but the Zhang Gong Dike was in a state of distress. After this trial, many problems were discovered. The current state of the Zhang Gong Dike: Although the Zhang Gong Dike was raised to 29.14 feet (average) in 1931, it was not thickened. The inner slope is extremely steep, and the dike body is weak. Moreover, the inner side is mostly lake, and the soil quality is soft. In recent years, during flood prevention, soil has been taken from the inner base of the dike, resulting in an extremely hollow dike foot. Every flood season, the inside and outside are a vast expanse of water, and the dike body collapses in weak areas. This situation occurred mostly in the Jintan and Yintan areas last year, but suddenly appeared in Gusaoshu, with a tragic scene. The dike soil layers peeled off and subsided, and the dike surface collapsed. Most of the areas were concentrated on emergency rescue. Other similar dangerous situations are too numerous to mention. Therefore, to increase the consolidation of the Zhang Gong Dike and ensure the safety of the city of Hankou, the Zhang Gong Dike must be widened, and the inner slope must be flattened to a slope of 1:5. The water on the inner side of the dike should be filled from the dike foot to a distance of 20 to 50 meters, and sufficient foundation work should be applied to ensure safety. Hankou city's circular dike defense. Construction plan and design standards: estimated according to two different standards: (A) Estimated at a height of 30.6 meters, the cost is 2,137,398 yuan, of which 900,000 yuan can be covered by public bonds. (B) Estimated at a height of 30.000 meters, the cost is 1,819,179 yuan, of which 900,000 yuan can be covered by public bonds. As for the allocation, the estimated cost for type A is: 361,800 yuan for the earthwork project of Zhang Gong Dike, 141,500 yuan for the renovation of the gentle slope project, 192,500 yuan for the masonry gentle slope project, 88,380 yuan for the earthwork project from Dijiao to Fenjinlu, 23,805 yuan for the reconstruction of the revetment project, 63,566 yuan for raising the revetment project, 21,120 yuan for the masonry pebble landslide project, a total of 196,871 yuan, and 27,597 yuan for the steel-concrete flood wall project in Lower Taikoo. The estimated cost for type B is: 173,700 yuan for the earthwork of Zhang Gong Dike, 74,000 yuan for the renovation of the gentle slope, 88,380 yuan for the earthwork from Dijiao to Fenjinlu, 23,805 yuan for the reconstruction of the revetment, 63,566 yuan for raising the revetment, and 21,120 yuan for the masonry landslide. Furthermore, the Hankou Municipal Government sent a letter to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau regarding the design standards of the Zhang Gong Dike. The dike body from Dijiao via Gusaoshu to Shuitang is raised to 61 feet. The inner slope is 1:2.5 below 2 meters from the dike surface and 1:5 below that. The water 20 meters from the dike foot is uniformly filled. The section from Dijiao to the sleeper factory is widened and raised on the outside of the original dike. The original stone gentle slope is completely demolished and rebuilt. The dike height is raised to 58.5 feet, the dike surface is 8 meters wide, and the inner slope and water filling are the same as above. Subsequently, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau replied with a proposed change plan. The Zhang Gong Dike from Dijiao to Daijiashan dike surface is 6 meters wide, the dike height is 58 feet, and the inner slope is changed to 1:3. From Daijiashan to the water plant, the dike surface is 8 meters wide, the dike height is 58 feet, and the inner slope is 1:3. The dike height is changed to 57 feet from Fenjinlu to Dijiao. The earthwork is requested to be handled by the people's service. As for the cost of adding revetments and gentle slope projects, and the flood wall along the river and in the Lower Taikoo area of Special Zone 1 and 2, there are no methods for raising funds for repairs. The municipal government believes that the flood season is approaching, and the dike repair project cannot be delayed. Therefore, it sent technician Wang Hualu to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau for liaison. According to the technician at the municipal government, "The Jianghan Engineering Bureau has been instructed by the National Economic Commission to take overall charge of the heightening of the Fenjinlu Dijiao revetment and the flood wall project in Special Zone 1 and 2 and Lower Taikoo. However, the total budget for annual repairs in the province this year is only 2 million yuan, while the estimated cost of the projects to be repaired is more than 2.49 million yuan. After approving 2 million yuan, there is still a shortfall of more than 490,000 yuan, which has been submitted to the Economic Commission for supplementary allocation. However, the cost of the revetment and flood control has not been estimated. Whether these projects can be built in the future depends on the results of the engineering bidding and whether there are any remaining funds. The bureau has not yet decided to build the flood wall and revetment projects. However, before the water level rose last year, the municipal government had proposed to allocate 80,000 yuan for the Zhang Gong Dike repair project and asked the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to handle it. The bureau used only 80,000 yuan for the repair project, resulting in flood control expenditures of more than 470,000 yuan due to the continuous rise in water levels. The total cost of repairing the entire dike this year is more than 1.8 million yuan. The bureau decided to divide the work into front and rear. The bureau is responsible for repairing the rear dike from Dijiao via Daijiashan Gusaoshu to Shuitang, which requires more than 300,000 yuan, now reduced to 220,000 yuan. The front is from Dijiao along the river to Qiaokou, which is handled by the municipal government at a cost of more than 1.4 million yuan. However, due to limited funds, it was decided to postpone the section from Jianghan Customs to Jukou and start work on the more urgent revetment project from Special Zone 1 and 2 in Lower Taikoo and Fenjinlu to Dijiao, which requires only more than 170,000 yuan, plus more than 20,000 yuan for civil service expenses, totaling more than 190,000 yuan. However, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau suddenly refused to allocate this amount, making it impossible to proceed with the above projects."

Xiang River Remote Dike

After the great flood of 1931, many of the dikes along the upper and lower reaches of the Xiang River in Hubei Province were breached. Although they were repaired afterward, they were not all completely restored. In 1935, another major flood completely breached the dikes in Hubei Province, which urgently needed to be repaired. After the plan for repairing the Xiang River Remote Dike at three or four work sites was determined, an engineering office was established, with Xi Dejiong, Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, concurrently serving as the Director. Commissioner Shi, County Magistrate Xiong, and others jointly summoned 80,000 workers from various Baojia to build the dikes in sections, with 50 people in each group. At present, most sections have started work, but the number of workers has not yet been fully recruited and is still being recruited. In addition, the Hubei Dike Fund Management Committee and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau borrowed 1 million yuan from five banks, including the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Farmers Bank of China, and the Provincial Bank of Hubei, to repair the Xiang River Remote Dike. The five banks promised to lend the full amount and immediately agreed on a draft, which will be signed and delivered soon. The contents are as follows: A guarantee is provided in the form of 1.5 million yuan face value of 1935 Flood Disaster Work-Relief Bonds and 400,000 yuan face value of Compilation and Dismissal Treasury Bonds. The interest rate is 9% per month. The principal will be repaid in full by the end of December of the 15th year (of the Republic). From April to September, 20,000 yuan will be repaid each month, and 300,000 yuan will be repaid in each of the months of October and November. 280,000 yuan will be repaid in December, matching the total amount of 1 million yuan. Interest will also be paid on schedule.

Tongren Dike

The Yangtze River Tongren Dike, which is related to the three provinces of Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui, has always been repaired by the three provinces sharing the costs equally. After the great flood last year, although the dike did not collapse, there were many defects. After the three provincial governments sent personnel to jointly survey with the personnel of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau in December last year, it was believed that the amount of earthwork to be moved for this repair should be doubled compared with the previous time. Whether the required funds should be allocated by the National Economic Commission or shared equally by the three provinces should be requested by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to the Economic Commission for instructions. Recently, instructions were received from the Economic Commission, stating that the funds for plugging breaches and restoring dikes have already been fully allocated. The three provinces of Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui should still share the costs equally to comply with the original plan. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau immediately submitted the number of funds required for the Tongren Dike repair project to the Hubei Provincial Government for verification. The total length of the dike repair project is 3.6 kilometers, requiring 342,000 cubic meters of earthwork. At a unit price of 1.8 cents per cubic meter, including ramming work, the project requires 61,560 yuan. The three provinces should each share equally, with each being responsible for 20,520 yuan. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau also suggested that the Hubei Provincial Government could deduct the amount to be shared by Anhui Province from the 18,810 yuan of the Hubei Province's share of the Ma Hua Dike project funds, and request that the amount to be shared by Jiangxi Province be allocated in full to facilitate the organization of an engineering office to start construction. Upon receiving the report, the Hubei Provincial Government specifically consulted the Jiangxi and Anhui Provincial Governments to act accordingly and ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to organize a temporary engineering office and start construction immediately.

Ma Hua Dike

The provinces of Jiangxi, Anhui, and Hubei have been jointly constructing the Ma Hua Dike for months and re-demarcating the borders of the three provinces. Regarding the construction of the Ma Hua Dike, after the three provincial governments consulted with each other through letters and telegrams and sent personnel to jointly survey, it has now been decided that the Ma Hua Dike will be constructed by the three provinces sharing the funds. The Department of Construction of Anhui Province will be in charge of the restoration project. The Hubei Provincial Government received a telegram from the Anhui Provincial Government requesting that the allocated engineering funds be remitted immediately to facilitate the start of construction. After receiving the telegram, the Hubei Provincial Government ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to allocate funds from the Hubei Dike funds for remittance to Anhui for application. It has now been decided that the Ma Hua Dike project will be presided over by the Department of Construction of Anhui Province. As for the required engineering funds, Hubei will pay 56%, Anhui will pay 31%, and Jiangxi will pay 13%. After the engineering fees are determined, personnel will be sent to survey and estimate and formulate a plan. Anhui Province is currently inviting bids for handling, and construction will start in the near future. As for the Ma Hua Dike, which is not within its borders, Hubei Province bears more engineering fees than Jiangxi and Anhui, which is in accordance with previous practice, because if the Ma Hua Dike is in danger, Hubei Province will be most affected. (You Shize, student of this newspaper's correspondence school)

Taicang: The Post Office Cracks Down on Ships Carrying Letters 80

Merchants and residents of this county still follow the old custom of entrusting letters to ships and other carriers. Yesterday, Chen Abing, a crew member of the Chen Mei Ji ship traveling between Suzhou and Taicang, brought more than 20 letters from Suzhou and was distributing them along the Beihong Lane in the city when he was discovered by Chen Zhenchou, the Director of the Taicang Post Office. Chen Abing was handed over to the police and taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It is said that the post office is cracking down on the private carrying of letters very strictly. However, this is the first time this has been heard of in this county, so the people are not aware of it.

Suzhou: Fierce General Competition Leads to Death 81

In the vicinity of Mu Du Tianping Mountain in Suzhou, villagers held a fierce general competition the other day. Unexpectedly, during the competition, a palanquin accidentally collided with villager Zhao Hongshou's chest, causing him to fall to the ground. Shortly after, he died of his injuries. The local Baotou reported the incident to the local procuratorate and requested that personnel be sent for inspection. The procuratorate immediately dispatched Prosecutor Lv to lead the police to the countryside on the 17th for inspection. After confirming that Zhao Hongshou had indeed died of his injuries, he returned to the court that evening. On the 18th, he issued summonses to Mao Tou, Liu Hugen, Fan Hesheng, Liu Fugen, and Zhao Hegao, the father of the deceased, to appear in court on the 19th for investigation. It is reported that the local Baojia has mediated the private prosecution, and the Fierce General Hall has contributed 150 yuan to cover funeral expenses. The public prosecution part is awaiting court trial.

Organizing a County Autonomy Research Association 82

Fan Junbozhuan, the township head of Dacheng Township in the first district of Wuxian County, who has been trained, submitted a request to the county party headquarters to establish a Wuxian County branch of the Jiangsu Trained Township Heads Alumni Association to promote autonomy and contact the township heads of various counties. The county party headquarters changed the name to Wuxian County Autonomy Research Association because the name was inconsistent and approved the organization and sent personnel to guide it. Fan Junbo and others immediately convened the initiators for a meeting and immediately elected Fan Junbo, Zhang Zhiming, and Ye Zhongliang and others as preparation members. They immediately began to solicit members in order to hold an inaugural meeting as soon as possible.

Public Security Bureau Repeatedly Arrests Bandits 83

On the morning of the 18th, the Criminal Investigation Team of the Public Security Bureau successively captured three bandits, Xiong Zhengxin, Lin Ajin, and Lin Awu, outside Chuangmen, and two bandits, Chen A and Lao Wen, at the Lao Gan Feng Inn on Xueshi Street in the city, and two bandits, Yi Zhenshan and Zheng Atang, and two female bandits, Yi Hushi and Zheng Yangshi, inside the Shui Zhu at No. 40 Chuanzhu Lane. A five-shot revolver, eleven bullets, and 300 yuan in stolen foreign currency were seized at Wangshu Dun. They were immediately taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

The Spread of Epidemics in Suzhou City 84

The weather here has been abnormal for several days. The highest temperature on the 17th was 59.5, and the lowest on the 18th was 38.5. The sudden warm and cold weather has led to the spread of epidemics and many deaths. Among the patients who went to various hospitals in the city for diagnosis and treatment, two cases of meningitis and more than ten cases of diphtheria were found. It is reported that most of the deaths are children. In addition, lung disease is rampant in the third sub-prison on Siqian Street. It is reported that inmates are still dying every day, and the rate is increasing. At most, four people die in one day, and at least two or three people die.

Changzhou: Suspension of New Prison Construction, Request to Build Detention Center 85

The Wuyi Prison was previously overcrowded, so the county government and the local court jointly identified a site in Yangyuan to build a new prison to expand the internal workshops and improve the conditions. However, due to land price issues, it has not been realized to date. However, all the construction budget and handling process have been submitted to the Higher Court and forwarded to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for review. According to information from the Ministry, the land price is too high, and the funds are insufficient. Now that the Wuxi New Prison has been built, long-term prisoners can be transferred to the new prison in that county. Therefore, the construction of the new prison in Jinting is not necessary and is ordered to be suspended. Weng Zushou, the warden of the detention center, stated that the first and second detention centers are located in two different places, making unified management impossible. In addition, the houses are dilapidated, making all administrative and security work very difficult. Since the construction of a new prison in Yangyuan cannot be realized, it is planned to build a new detention center on the vacant land next to the procuratorate within the local court. The funds are requested to be allocated from the thousands of yuan previously donated and deposited, and the local court is requested to forward the request for an allocation of 10,000 yuan for construction expenses in the 25th year's budget to enable the construction to be carried out.

Yangzhou: Construction of Grassland Park in the North of the City 86

The Management Committee of the Scenic Area in the North of the City previously decided to build a grassland park in the area of Sanmaogong in the North Gate. However, the thatched houses in the vicinity of the site have been ordered by the county government to be vacated within a time limit, but the residents there have not yet complied, causing many obstacles to the progress of the work. Yesterday, it specifically sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, ordering the police to order all residents from the North Gate city gate to the elevated mounds directly on the eastern First Fortress to completely vacate the area within two weeks. In addition, the boundary of the scenic area has also been determined. The east side temporarily starts from Guangchumen, along the city moat, the Caohe River, to Baozhang Lake. The west side temporarily starts from Ximen, passing through the Twenty-Four Bridges to the Situ Temple. Yesterday, it also sent a letter to the Provincial Yangzhou Middle School, requesting the dispatch of engineering students to conduct measurements from March 1st and prepare a 1:1000 scale plan to facilitate project implementation.

Canal Bureau Merges Three Offices 87

The Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau, after a resolution by the provincial government meeting, reduced the red fees, moved to Huaiyin, and changed the three section engineering offices of Jiangdu, Gaobao, and Huai Pi into upstream and downstream. The upstream office is stationed in Suqian, and the downstream office is stationed in Gaoyou. Qi An, an engineer from the Lianshui Engineering Office of the Guidance of Huai River into the Sea Project, has been appointed as the director of the downstream office of the Jiang, Shi, and Jia projects. Wang Zizun, the former director of the Jiangdu section, and Li Shiyuan, the director of the Gao Saizun section, have been transferred to be inspectors of the Canal Jiang Bureau. As for who will be the director of the upstream office, it has not yet been determined. The date of the move of the River Works Bureau itself has not been determined. It is said that it will be moved north on March 1st, and the bureau address will be temporarily attached to the Guidance of Huai River into the Sea Project.

Nantong: Disabled Veterans Arrive in Nantong to Learn Skills 88

The Ministry of Military Affairs provides relief to disabled veterans of the National Army who fought against bandits and has specially converted the poor people's workshop in the west of the city into the Nantong Military Factory, appointing Wang Dayin as the factory director. Wounded soldiers from various provinces and regions will be transported to Nantong in batches to learn skills in the factory. Local News

Yesterday Morning in the Yuawo Sand Waters: The Xin Jiangtian Steamer Collides with a Sailing Ship - The Sailing Ship, Fully Loaded with Oil Barrels, Sinks Immediately - All Twenty Men and Women on Board are Missing 89

Central News Agency reports that the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Jiangtian Steamer, which was sailing from Ningbo to Shanghai yesterday morning, collided with a sailing ship near Yuawo Sand outside Wusong Estuary, sinking it. All the old and young men and women on board were reported missing. According to reporters, the details are as follows:

Xin Jiangtian Steamer Passes Through Yuawo Sand

The Xin Jiangtian Steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company specializes in sailing between Shanghai and Ningbo. It was sailing from Ningbo to Shanghai yesterday morning. At about 4:40 AM, it approached Block House Bony (Yuawo Sand area). Because a cargo ship was anchored and moored on the left side of the steamer's route, the steamer had to steer to continue forward. Unexpectedly, at that time, a large sailing ship, fully loaded with oil barrels, was sailing in with its sails up. After the steamer noticed it, it quickly changed its direction and sounded its whistle to warn the sailing ship. However, at that time, the northeast wind was strong, and the sailing ship was difficult to control. As a result, the steamer and the sailing ship collided. The hull of the sailing ship was immediately cut off, causing seawater to rush in, and the sailing ship immediately sank.

Sailing Ship Destroyed, Impossible to Rescue

At the time of the accident, the Xin Jiangtian Steamer was on duty by the first mate Yu Tingyuan and the second mate Gong Daohai. The captain of the steamer, a Norwegian named T.H. Johnson, was about to go to the bridge to be on duty because the steamer was approaching Yuawo Sand outside the Wusong Estuary. When he heard the sound of the collision, he knew that an accident had occurred. He rushed up to observe and saw only a few oil barrels and the destroyed wooden ship floating in the white waves. He then lowered the sampan and tried to rescue the crew members. But all the sailors, old and young men and women, of the destroyed ship had disappeared. Rescuing for an hour had no effect, so he immediately steamed the steamer to Shanghai to report the incident to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company.

Captain Johnson Reports the Incident

Captain Johnson reported the accident to the Ship Section of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Customs and Port Authority. The following is a translation of the letter to the director of the Ship Section: Director of the Ship Section: At 5:00 AM this morning, my steamer was entering the port and sailing through Yuawo Sand when a huge collision sound suddenly occurred. I immediately rushed to the bridge to observe and discovered that it was a collision with a huge sailing ship. At that time, my steamer was sailing forward at full speed. I immediately ordered the rudder to be turned to the right to avoid colliding with another anchored ship. Afterward, I turned the ship around to search. At about 6:00 AM, I discovered the destroyed sailing ship about one mile east of Yuawo Sand. However, there were no people floating. The sailors and crew members of the ship may have been rescued by other passing ships, or they may have drowned. The first and second mates of my steamer were both on duty at the time. Johnson, Captain of the Xin Jiangtian Steamer, February 18.

First and Second Mates Report to the Maritime Affairs Bureau

The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau received the report of the Xin Jiangtian Steamer's accident yesterday. The original text reads: Respectfully submitted, at 4:45 AM this morning, my steamer was sailing from Ningbo to Shanghai and arrived at Block House Bony (near Yuawo Sand). The weather was dark, the sky was covered with dark clouds, and the northeast wind was extremely strong. We were driving carefully and proceeding forward. At that time, a cargo ship was anchored and moored slightly to the left of my steamer's route. Unexpectedly, a sailing ship appeared on the right side of my steamer's bow. I immediately changed the direction of the steamer and warned the sailing ship with the whistle and stopped the engine to avoid the sailing ship. But it was too late. The hull of the sailing ship was slightly grazed. Because the ship had a heavy load, it sank due to the water seeping into the ship. The sailing ship did not have running lights, and the equipment on board was inadequate. Although my steamer stopped the engine and searched, only a few oil barrels were seen floating on the surface of the water. There were no crew members seen, and there was nothing that could be done. Therefore, we had to enter the port and dock. I respectfully submit the details of the incident. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, Yu Tingyuan, First Mate. Gong Daohai, Second Mate. February 18. As for the sailing ship's side, there has been no report received by the bureau.

No Report from the Sailing Ship's Side

According to reporters, the Xin Jiangtian Steamer left Ningbo at about 5:00 PM the day before yesterday. On the Zhenhai Port surface, it ran aground. It escaped the danger after a violent drive and continued on its way to Shanghai. It was safe on the way. Only the rudder blade was slightly damaged. Unexpectedly, when it reached the Yuawo Sand outside the Wusong Estuary, the tragedy still occurred. Although the steamer was not damaged, the sinking of the sailing ship resulted in the loss of all the crew members on board, which is extremely unfortunate. Although the Maritime Affairs Bureau has received the report from the Xin Jiangtian Steamer, the sailing ship's side has not yet reported to the bureau, so it is very difficult to handle the matter. Yesterday, only the captain of the steamer, Johnson, was briefly questioned. It is said that there were as many as 20 men and women missing from the sailing ship.

Xu Shiying to Go to Japan Next Month to Take Office, According to Reports, Foreign Policy Towards Japan Will Follow the Central Government's Guidelines, Seeking Solutions Under Mutual Respect for Sovereignty 92

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the newly appointed Ambassador to Japan, Xu Shiying, returned to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning and is scheduled to go to Japan to take office in early next month. The trip to Huangshan has been canceled due to time constraints. The details are as follows:

Foreign Policy Towards Japan

Yesterday, Mr. Xu stated in his reply to the Xin Xin News Agency reporter at the station that his views on his mission to Japan have been detailed in his remarks issued in Beijing and need not be repeated. After taking office, he will adhere to the established foreign policy of the Central Government and seek appropriate solutions to various difficult issues between the two countries in the past under the principle of mutual respect for sovereignty in order to promote the increasing advancement of friendly relations between the two countries. He hopes that all wise men will help him overcome his shortcomings so that he can fulfill his duties and not disgrace his mission.

To Take Office Next Month

I originally planned to leave for my post abroad as early as the 25th, but because Ambassador Arida still has a field and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from Japan on the 26th, I have decided to postpone my departure until early next month so that I can meet with Mr. Arida before taking office.

Huangshan Trip Cancelled

According to Secretary Huang Bodu, Mr. Xu told the Xin Xin News Agency reporter that Ambassador Xu's trip to Huangshan has been canceled because he is about to take office and time is short. After completing his social engagements in Shanghai, he will enter Beijing again on the evening of the 19th to meet with Chairman Lin of the National Government for instructions and continue to bid farewell to President Jiang, Foreign Minister Zhang, etc., and receive his credentials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs before returning to Shanghai to wait for the ship to go to Japan. In addition to myself and staff member Hu Mai, Wang Pengsheng, the newly appointed Counselor of the Embassy, will also travel with Ambassador Xu. As for when Acting Ambassador Ding Shaoji, who has been recalled home, will depart from Japan, no telegram has yet been received. It is expected that he will start his journey home after Ambassador Xu arrives in Japan.

The content is edited by the association and the materials are quite rich. Today, major newspapers will meet readers with this special edition. The Party Voice, published by the City Party Department, will also issue a special edition and distribute it to the representatives attending the meeting.

Cai's Opinion

Cai Jinjun published an article entitled "The New Life Movement and Police Training," stating that the New Life Movement is the foundation of a new life for our Chinese nation. Its purpose is to transform the inherent virtues of our nation, such as propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, into rules of daily life for the people, and to promote inner construction through external training. This is a good medicine for the current environment and pathological state of our nation. Since Chairman Jiang proposed and implemented it, it has been the second anniversary.

Page 12

In the past two years, the whole country has followed suit, and there has been a rapid rise in momentum. Judging from the facts, both quality and quantity have achievements to be proud of. However, for further requirements, it is necessary to deeply penetrate this rule and virtue into the national consciousness and become a common practice, so that it will be done without being ordered, and there will be no fear of intermittent cessation. To achieve this requirement, police training is an urgent task. The position and responsibility of the police are directly related to the people. Not only in the passive aspect should they spare no effort to maintain social stability, but also in the active aspect should they use moral strength to transform social customs. If they can set an example and have the norms of a teacher and nanny, then the people will have something to emulate, and the effect will be obvious. Since the establishment of the New Life Movement Section in this bureau in April last year, the training of senior police officers has been the most important basic work in the first phase. It is planned to give all of them New Life Movement training, teach the New Life Movement outline and New Life Movement essentials, and explain the various matters for the police themselves to practice the New Life Movement. The New Life Movement Section sends personnel to each branch, station, and team to teach, and also formulates an implementation schedule for the New Life Movement training for senior police officers, which is advancing according to the schedule. The first phase of training has violated one-third of all senior police officers, and the remaining two-thirds will continue to be trained in the second phase, with the goal of completing the matter in the shortest possible time. However, the importance of the police promoting the New Life Movement has been mentioned above, and it seems that it is not enough to issue it as a decree and promulgate it throughout the country to provide universality and show unity. If the Ministry of Interior orders all police agencies across the country to list the promotion of the New Life Movement as one of the formal duties, and at the same time, the local New Life Movement Promotion Association closely liaises with the local police agencies, unifies the steps, and details the implementation plan, then the future of the New Life Movement should be able to make greater progress. My humble opinion is that the relevant authorities of the Ministry of Interior and those responsible for promoting the New Life Movement should discuss and decide, then it would be fortunate.

In addition to Ambassador to Japan Xu Shiying and Ambassador to France Gu Weijun, the representatives of the various groups who attended the farewell tea party yesterday included Xu Jiyin, Lin Kanghou, Huang Bodu, Xu Xinliu, Zai Yingbin, Dong Xianguang, Wu Yunzhai, Yu Qiaqing, Tang Zaifu, Xi Jimin, Guo Bingwen, Qian Xinzhi, Li Denghui, Li Zhaohuan, Luo Qinghua, Lu Yigeng, Zhou Zuomin, Miao Zhongxiu, Zou Bingwen, Chen Guangfu, Yang Yihui, Yu Zuoting, Lu Ganchen, Wang Chuntao, Wang Xiaolai, Lu Bohong, Wang Shouxian, Ding Huikang, Zhu Shaoping, Ou Zhaotang, Ke Zhenxin, Guo Zefan, and more than 100 others.

Delivering Farewell Speech

Chairman Guo Bingwen delivered a farewell speech, saying that today the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Local Association, Money Industry Association, Banking Association, International Trade Association, Taxpaying Chinese Association, International Issues Research Association, University Federation, Pacific International Society, Youth Association, Catholic Action Association, and Global Chinese Student Association and other 12 groups are jointly holding a farewell to Ambassadors Gu and Xu. It is a great honor for Ambassadors Gu and Xu to attend in their busy schedules. Everyone knows about the two gentlemen's academic experience and contributions to society and the country. There is no need for introduction. Moreover, everyone knows the moral qualifications of the two gentlemen and the spirit of responsible handling of affairs. Ambassador Xu's visit to Japan, we are very fortunate to adjust the relationship between China and Japan, will certainly work hard. Ambassador Gu's visit to France will further promote the friendship between China and France in the future. Therefore, the colleagues are sincerely bidding farewell to the two gentlemen's departure. Some people say that weak countries have no diplomacy. At the same time, the diplomatic staff also feel the difficulties and hardships of weak countries. In fact, weak countries do not have no diplomacy. I just hate that there is no certain diplomatic policy and no certain diplomatic method. Today, the two gentlemen's missions are very different from the past. We stand on the position of the people and hope to work hard for the future of the nation and the country.

Xu's Reply

Ambassador to Japan Xu Shiying then stood up and gave a reply, saying, "Chairman, ladies and gentlemen, I am very grateful for the kindness of all my old friends today. The chairman's words about Shiying are even more praiseworthy, which I dare not accept. Shiying has been in Shanghai for more than ten years. He has been loved and guided and assisted by local officials and outsiders on weekdays. He is willing to solicit for charity, and he is enthusiastic and ambitious for many years as one day. Apart from private friendship, in terms of public friendship, he is really reluctant to part and reluctant to separate. Although Shiying is old, he is still a young junior in the diplomatic world. Today, Ambassador Gu and all of you here are advanced people. I hope to give guidance, and I hope that all parties will give advice at any time. However, Shiying's talent is limited, and he feels fearful to shoulder such a heavy responsibility. He only has the patriotism and sincerity to follow Confucius's instruction of not disgracing his mission and strive to do it in order to be worthy of the government and the people. Today, all of you here are social leaders and have a deep understanding and research on international politics and economics. Everything still depends on your instructions. A thousand miles of book, I hope you will be happy. I wish you all good health. Thank you all."

Gu's Reply

Chairman, ladies and gentlemen, just now the chairman gave a farewell speech, which was extremely encouraging and humbling. Today, the 12 groups held such a grand tea party to bid farewell to Ambassadors Xu and Weijun. In addition to gratitude, I am really reluctant to say goodbye to the kindness of all of you. Today, Ambassador Xu's mission to Japan is of great concern to all of you, and Weijun, who is going to Europe, is also very concerned. Ambassador Xu's difficulty is different from Weijun's. However, our diplomacy is based on the people. Today, all of you are the leaders of various groups. I hope you will contribute more guidance. At present, the friendly relations between China and France have reached a very good stage. The French have always been rich in artistic ideas. Although our country is very old, it also likes art very much. The French love peace, and we also love peace. Therefore, with the similarities in the national character of the two countries, we can further promote the friendship between the two countries, which will naturally become better and better. However, the 25th year of the Republic of China is not only very tense in the Far East, but also in Europe. After Weijun goes abroad, I hope that all of you present today will give more guidance. Then, the meeting broke up and talked freely until about 7 o'clock.

Stock Exchange Opened One Session Yesterday Afternoon, Suspension of Trading in the Morning Due to Complicated Procedures for Recovering Certificates and Withdrawing Cash 96

After the Chinese Stock Exchange was ordered by the Ministry of Finance to open the market the day before yesterday, the prices of various bonds fell, and trading was suspended yesterday morning to recover the security deposit and submit the spot goods. After the board of directors meeting in the afternoon, it was decided to open trading at 4:30 pm, still doing one session. Except for the omissions, the various bonds were all down. The Ministry has stipulated the date for the exchange of unified public bonds. The details are as follows:

Suspension of Trading Yesterday Morning

Recover Spot Goods

The Chinese Stock Exchange suspended trading yesterday morning and issued a notice to recover the spot goods. The announcement is recorded as follows: "It is found that the futures trading in February, the seller's deposit account of each broker, will be ordered by the Ministry of Finance Qian Zi No. 22078, and should be submitted in spot goods. The market has been notified by the exchange's announcement No. 2243, and the Brokers Association has been notified by letter to all brokers on the 15th. However, some brokers have not yet paid. Now, after the resolution of the 16th board of directors meeting on the 17th, it is limited to 12 noon on the 18th to submit to the exchange. The buyer's recovery of gold is also limited to 12 noon on the 18th. If it cannot be paid on time, the exchange will handle it according to the business rules. In addition to the circular, I hope you will follow it and do not delay. Special announcement."

Board of Directors Meeting

Change to One Session

At 2 pm yesterday afternoon, the exchange held a board of directors meeting. The directors Zhang Weiru, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Malian, Chen Duoru, and Zhou Shouliang attended. After Chairman Zhang Weiru reported, it was decided to change to one session at 4:30 pm. It was only dismissed at about 3 pm. That is, the exchange announced that "Today's Shan business meeting decided that because the procedures for recovering security deposit and submitting spot goods are complicated and time is not enough, it should be changed to one session, scheduled to open at 4:30 pm. Special announcement."

Open Trading in the Afternoon

Less Falls and More Rises

It was only finished at about 5 pm. Shanghai Municipal Police Department Intensifies Anti-Smoking Efforts: Roster Compilation Completed, Plans for Phased Reduction, Regular Inspections, and Severe Punishment for Relapsed Smokers 98

According to Da Gong She, the Shanghai Municipal Police Department, since the registration of opium smokers at the end of last December, subsequently received an order from Inspector-General Chiang, stipulating that the registration situation and detailed number of opium smokers be submitted for review within January of this year. Therefore, the Opium Smoker Registration Section of the department immediately began compiling a roster and conducting separate statistics. However, due to the excessive number of registered individuals, exceeding 37,000, and the need for detailed classification, it could not be completed immediately. The section then increased personnel to actively compile the opium smoker roster, which is now largely complete. In addition to the master roster, separate statistics are compiled for ordinary poor people regarding their age, origin, occupation, reasons for smoking, quantity smoked, years of smoking, registration date, deadline for cessation, etc., in extreme detail. After review and verification in the coming days, it will be submitted to the Anti-Smoking Inspector-General and published in a compiled form. Simultaneously, in accordance with this statistic, a phased reduction plan is being meticulously discussed.

Intensified Investigation: The department originally registered over 5,000 opium smokers who were unable to obtain permits and applied for rehabilitation. Subsequently, due to intensified investigation efforts, the number of opium smokers apprehended daily reached double digits, leading to overcrowding. The existing opium addiction treatment hospitals in various districts were insufficient to accommodate them. To alleviate the suffering of opium smokers and expedite addiction treatment, the department specifically increased beds in opium addiction treatment hospitals for offenders in both the southern and northern Shanghai areas, reaching a total of 1,080 beds, to accelerate treatment. As a result, the number of opium smokers undergoing treatment gradually decreased. Currently, over 5,000 individuals have been discharged after completing treatment, and the number awaiting treatment is small and will soon be completed, it is said.

Strict Enforcement Ordered: Anti-Smoking Inspector-General Chiang, in order to ensure that all

regions earnestly handle opium smoker registration without omissions, and to provide guidelines for reporting, previously telegraphed all provinces and municipalities to comply. The municipal government yesterday forwarded the order to the Public Security Bureau for implementation. An excerpt of the original telegram is as follows (omitted above): Investigations into registration in various provinces show that Jiangsu's performance is relatively superior. Although the total number of registered opium smokers in Jiangsu is nearly 200,000, the accuracy remains to be verified. The number of registered opium smokers reported by other provinces and municipalities is very small, and omissions are feared to be more difficult to avoid. Hereafter, the yearly cessation of smoking and the quantity of domestically produced raw materials purchased by border provinces should all use this national total of registered opium smokers as the standard. If the number reported by each province and municipality does not match the actual number, then the entire anti-smoking design will be affected. To ensure widespread and accurate registration, the concurrently serving Inspector-General convened the first standing committee meeting of the Anti-Smoking Commission to discuss practical solutions, and specifically established fourteen articles for reporting opium smokers to be implemented, urging compliance and strict enforcement. No further excuses for extension will be tolerated. After this reporting, if there are still oversights or omissions, they will be treated as dereliction of duty and dealt with accordingly (omitted below), etc.

Deadline for Permit Renewal: Since receiving the telegram from Inspector-General Chiang, in addition to planning to comply with the reporting methods to report opium smokers, the department decided to complete the renewal of official permits for registered opium smokers in this city and permits for opium smokers traveling to Shanghai from other regions within this month. Hereafter, opium smokers coming to Shanghai, regardless of the duration of their stay, should apply to the department for permit renewal at any time, and a public notice has been issued to that effect. Once the permit renewal procedures are completed, the department will begin preparing for random inspections to check whether each permit holder is earnestly quitting smoking and whether opium smokers who have quit are relapsing. At that time, those found not to have quit smoking within the deadline will be severely punished according to law. As for those found to have relapsed, first-time offenders will be sentenced to imprisonment for up to six months, second-time offenders will be sentenced to imprisonment for more than three years, and third-time offenders will be executed by shooting to deter incorrigible individuals, it is said.

Extension of Registration: According to Shen Shi She, the Shanghai Special Trades Association previously requested the municipal government to petition the Chairman of the Military Commission and concurrently serving Anti-Smoking Inspector-General to extend the opium smoker registration period to ensure its widespread nature, as there were many omissions in opium smoker registration. This has now been approved by Chairman Chiang, who instructed the municipal government to instruct the Shanghai Special Trades Association to allow unregistered opium smokers to voluntarily apply for registration during the reporting period. The municipal government's instructions are recorded as follows: The municipal government instructs the Shanghai Special Trades Association, "According to the instructions from the Chairman of the Military Commission and concurrently serving Anti-Smoking Inspector-General, Order No. Jinzheng 65, which states, 'A case presented on December 16, 24th year, File No. 503, reporting that the Shanghai Special Trades Association reported special circumstances in the city and requested an extension of the opium smoker registration period, requesting review and instructions. The report is noted. It is stated that there are indeed over 100,000 opium smokers in the city. Currently, due to various special circumstances, the number of registered opium smokers is less than 30,000. It is requested that the registration period be extended to achieve widespread registration, etc.' While under review, a report from the municipal government on the number of registered opium smokers in the city lists only slightly over 30,000. Comparing the two reports, there are clearly many omissions. Now, registration reporting methods are being stipulated. During the reporting period, unregistered opium smokers are allowed to voluntarily apply for registration, reissue permits, and be exempt from punishment. They should wait for the dispatch of personnel to conduct joint reporting to ensure its widespread nature, ensuring that no opium smokers are omitted. This is of utmost importance. This order, etc., is received and should be complied with. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau, this order is issued for the association to be notified. This order."

Baoshan Opium Smokers' Self-Renewal Registration Closed Yesterday 99

Number Exceeds Six Hundred... Provincial Government Committee Member Ning's Talk

The opium smokers' self-renewal registration closed yesterday. The reporter specifically visited the residence of Mr. Ning Bojin, the Provincial Government Committee Member, and received the following remarks: "Our county is small in land and population. The initial estimate for unlicensed opium smokers was only two to three hundred. However, as of yesterday, the number of registered individuals actually reached over six hundred, which was completely unexpected. Based on this estimate, the total number for all sixty-one counties in the province should exceed one hundred thousand. Therefore, this self-renewal registration is a major key to the province's strict anti-smoking efforts. Over the past week, thanks to the enthusiastic assistance of all parties in the Party and government, and under the supervision and leadership of County Magistrate Zhang and Section Chief Fang, most have been working tirelessly, without leisure. This spirit of loyal service for society, the Party, the country, and the nation is truly admirable and commendable. Moreover, the majority of opium smokers have realized the miscalculation of being mired in the black market for so long, resolutely breaking away from the sea of suffering, and actively renewing themselves, which is sufficient to prove that there are indeed many heroic individuals among opium smokers. Now that the final reporting period is approaching, it is hoped that they will redouble their initial intentions and continue their efforts to achieve the goal of "thoroughly eradicating without omission." This will not only be fortunate for the future of anti-smoking policies, but will also make a great contribution to the revival of the national state," he said.

Shanghai Federation of Associations Urges Taxpayer Meeting on Telephone Issue Yesterday, Sends Representatives to Protest to Municipal Council Board of Directors Regarding Adoption of User Suggestions, Requests Post Office to Set Up Messenger Service 102

According to Xin Sheng She, the Shanghai First Special District Federation of Associations sent another letter to the Chinese and Foreign Ratepayers Association yesterday, requesting that a serious protest be lodged with the Municipal Council Board of Directors regarding the telephone rate increase issue. The original letter states: "To whom it may concern, the Shanghai Telephone Company's disguised telephone rate increase plan will be implemented from March 1st. At a time when the market is extremely depressed and we are already finding it difficult to maintain, how can we bear further burdens? Although the Telephone Issue Committee and various public organizations have repeatedly argued on reasonable grounds, the company has refused to accept them, resulting in no outcome. With implementation imminent, without a final sacrifice, we will inevitably continue to suffer destruction. At the joint meeting of representatives from various districts convened by this association a few days ago, it was resolved to nominate five representatives, Li Ao Kui, Yu Yaoqiu, Chen Jiufeng, Zhang Yizhai, Chen Youyun, etc., to negotiate with the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the concession, requesting that a taxpayer meeting be convened immediately, and to lodge a serious protest with the Municipal Council Board of Directors. We hereby record and convey this to your association, hoping that your association, representing the public opinion of taxpayers, will handle this matter promptly to comfort the public's hopes. Time is pressing, please take charge for the public's convenience."

Dispatching Representatives: Since the Shanghai Telephone Company announced that the new regulations would be implemented from March 1st, various groups in the city have risen up in opposition. The Special District Telephone Issue Committee has scheduled a joint meeting of all public organizations in the city for the 20th of this month to discuss the entire plan. In addition, the First Special District Federation of Associations, as a citizen group, attaches even greater importance to the rate increase plan. It has specifically nominated five committee members, Li Ao Kui, Yu Yaoqiu, Chen Jiufeng, Chen Youyun, and Zhang Yizhai, at the recent fourth plenary session of representatives, to represent the association in negotiating with the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the concession, requesting that a taxpayer meeting be convened to determine the solution, and to lodge a protest with the Municipal Council Board of Directors. It is learned that the representatives are scheduled to gather at the association at 1:00 PM today to depart, and the Ratepayers Association has been notified yesterday to designate a responsible representative to receive them, it is said.

User Suggestions: The Federation of Associations received suggestions from telephone users forwarded by the Seventh District, Fifth District, 27th District, 12th District, and 30th District branches, requesting that they be forwarded to the Ministry of Communications to instruct the Postal Administration to organize a messenger service in each postal district, regardless of distance, charging a uniform fee of one cent, before the telephone rate increase issue is resolved. The District Telephone Issue Committee submitted this to the representative assembly of various groups to discuss solutions, it is said.
