China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Issues Regulations on Rectifying Steamships by Order of the Executive Yuan, Notice Posted on Each Ship, Employee Examination Completed Yesterday 109

State-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, by order of the Executive Yuan, issued three regulations on rectifying steamships, and the notice has been posted on each ship. The employee examination was completed yesterday, and the written examination is scheduled for the 23rd. Details are recorded below.

Rectifying Passenger Ships: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, by order of the Executive Yuan, stipulated three regulations on rectifying the steamships on each route: Strictly prohibit stewards from extorting tips for wine. Suppress military personnel and public officials riding ships without tickets. Crew members are not allowed to carry smuggled goods. If found, they will be severely punished. The notice has been printed, signed by President of the Executive Yuan Chiang Chung-cheng, and countersigned by Yu Feipeng, Acting Minister of the Ministry of Communications. It has been distributed by the General Affairs Section to each ship for posting.

Examination Completed: Regarding employee examinations, after the examination committee members, including Lu Hanqin, repeatedly explained to the employees, the employees have expressed their acceptance. At 4:30 pm the day before yesterday, individual interviews, i.e., oral examinations, were conducted. The examination continued yesterday morning at 9:00 am, and by 5:00 pm, all employees of the General Affairs, Business, Shipping, and Accounting sections had completed the interviews. The written examination is scheduled to be held at the Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road at 9:00 am on the 23rd.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Instructs That Goods Received Books Should Have Stamps Affixed, Attendance Books Exempt 112

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied to Hesheng Fuji Company yesterday regarding doubts about the use of stamps, stating, "To whom it may concern, we received your letter of the 17th of this month inquiring about the use of stamp tax. Our reply is as follows: There is a distinction between internal and external receipts. Account books are purely for internal audit purposes and have no direct relationship with external parties. The Ministry of Finance has repeatedly explained this, so the affixing of stamps to account books is determined by whether they are related to business operations. Article 16, Item 11 of the Stamp Tax Law has long been stipulated. Stores rely on goods for business operations, and goods received books cannot be said to be unrelated to business operations and should be affixed with stamps according to law. An attendance book for employees, recording when they leave the store and when they return, has been approved by the Ministry of Finance and does not need to be affixed with stamps, it is said.

Eurasia Giant Aircraft Blindly Flew to Chengdu in Heavy Fog Yesterday Morning; Safely Arrived in Chengdu at 5:00 PM 124

Since the evening of the 16th, this city suddenly experienced spring fog due to the passage of a central low-pressure system. The fog gradually dissipated at 10:00 AM the day before yesterday (the 17th). However, at 2:30 AM yesterday, heavy fog returned, even heavier than before. The entire city was shrouded in fog, making it impossible to distinguish objects beyond five steps. As a result, both sea and air routes were delayed. China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong-Kunming southbound flight was delayed until 10:30 AM yesterday. However, according to an investigation by a China East News Agency reporter with Eurasia Aviation Corporation yesterday, the company's Xi'an-Chengdu northbound flight (the Junkers Ju 52 type first giant aircraft) was still able to take off from Longhua Airport at 6:30 AM as usual, despite the heavy fog. According to company personnel, the aircraft was equipped with blind flight instruments, allowing it to ascend into the fog and continue towards the capital in the absence of visual references. It took off at 6:30 AM, arrived in the capital at 7:50 AM, passed Zhengzhou at 10:45 AM, and safely arrived at Chengdu City Rock Phoenix Airport at 5:05 PM. It was only a few minutes off the company's scheduled time. It is said that this is the first time our national civil aviation has taken such a risk.

Total Number of Crimes Committed by Japanese Residents in This City Last Year: 703 Cases 125

The Japanese newspaper *Shanghai Nichi Nichi Shimbun* reports that the Legal Affairs Section of the Japanese Consulate-General's Police Department has completed its investigation report on the number of crimes committed by Japanese residents last year, totaling 703 cases involving 42 types of offenses. Among these 700-plus cases, 424 were violations of consulate orders that were immediately adjudicated, 133 were adjudicated as theft, 29 were violations of departmental orders, 24 were fraud, 14 were embezzlement in the course of business, 13 were assault, 10 were encroachment, 3 were murder, 1 was homicide, and 5 were robbery. In terms of reporting success, 587 of the 703 cases were reported, and 116 were not. The majority of these offenders were store employees and unemployed individuals. The motivation for the crimes was mostly attributed to frequenting entertainment venues such as cafes, restaurants, and dance halls, as well as engaging in gambling activities such as horse racing and dog racing, which led to poverty.

Detective Accused of Soliciting Bribes: Court Concludes Hearing, Verdict Pending 127

Wu Debao from Jurong, a cart leader residing in Changzhong Road, Zhabei, filed a lawsuit with the District Court Prosecutor's Office against Chen Hongsheng, Xia Liusheng, He Houchang, and several unidentified detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Police, alleging that they came to search his house on September 17 of last year, claiming that they had received a tip-off that the plaintiff was involved in a post office robbery case. After the search yielded nothing, Xia Liusheng instructed the plaintiff to meet him at a bathhouse on Xinzha Road the next day. The plaintiff went to the bathhouse as instructed and first met Wu Xueheng from Funing, a known sanitation inspector, who acted as an intermediary. As a result, the plaintiff was ordered to pay 20 yuan to settle the matter. The plaintiff paid 6 yuan in legal tender and 20 cents for the bath fee, with the remaining 14 yuan to be paid on December 2. However, when the due date arrived, Wu Xueheng came to demand payment. Feeling unwilling, the plaintiff reported the incident to the North Sichuan Road Police Station. Wu Xueheng was arrested, along with detectives Chen Hongsheng, Xia Liusheng, He Houchang, and others, and they were all transferred to the court for investigation and prosecution. It is now learned that Prosecutor Ouyang Shu has thoroughly investigated this case and filed a public prosecution for the crime of soliciting bribes. At 3:00 PM yesterday, Judge Chen Kangsun presided over the hearing in the Eleventh Tribunal. The plaintiff, Wu Debao, testified in court. When questioned, the defendants Xia Liusheng, Chen Hongsheng, He Houchang, and Wu Xueheng all denied soliciting bribes. The judge found the case to be clear and invited Prosecutor Ouyang to the court to present his opinion. Finally, the defendants' lawyers rose to defend them for a long time. The judge deemed the hearing concluded and awaited a scheduled verdict. The defendants were still released on bail. This is truly a vivid drama of a relative visit turning into a quarrel.

Impersonating a Military Officer: Fraud Case Concluded, Verdict Scheduled for the 25th 129

On the 3rd of this month, the Wuhan Garrison Command cracked down on fifteen individuals in Hankou, including Yu Hu and Wang Ziqi, who were impersonating members of the Hunan-Hubei-Sichuan Bandit Suppression Army. On the afternoon of the 7th, Yang Fengqi and Xu Pengfei, chiefs of the Songhu Garrison Command, along with the French police, went to the address and arrested Dong Yuyu from Fuyang, who was impersonating a brigade commander; Yu Hou from Longyou, who was impersonating a quartermaster; and Zhang Xueli from Shangyu, who was impersonating a staff officer. They also seized forged official documents, credentials, symbols, and correspondence. They were sent to the Second Special Court for questioning. After investigation, the French Police Affairs Department prosecuted the three individuals for disrupting order under Article 156 and using forged official documents under Articles 211 and 216. Wang Dongyu was also charged with fraud under Article 339. The Songhu Garrison Command sent personnel to the case and requested that they be transferred for investigation. Yesterday morning, they were interrogated again. Dong Yuyu claimed that he had been deceived by Wang Biao, who was at large, and that he had not recruited soldiers or sold credentials in the French Concession. He only realized that he was impersonating an officer when he was arrested. Yu confessed that he had been invited to Shanghai by his former classmate Yu Hu and had gone to Hankou with the other fifteen to wait to go to the front lines. He returned to Shanghai to urge them and had citizens advance over three thousand yuan. Zhang confessed that when he received the official document after being invited to Shanghai by Yu, he paid Wang 30 yuan as a service fee. The judge declared the debate concluded and scheduled the verdict for the 25th. The defendants were remanded in custody.

Therefore, she sent a letter to inform her parents, who came to Shanghai on the 13th of this month and went to her in-laws' house to visit. They were ordered to be released on bail pending further investigation. Yesterday, they were interrogated again. Mao Jinwen stated that after receiving his daughter's letter, he rushed to Shanghai to visit his daughter at his in-laws' house. Unexpectedly, his mother-in-law not only refused to welcome them, but also dared to speak disrespectfully, then slapped him several times and attempted to kill him with a knife. They claimed that the knife presented to the court was brought by the in-laws themselves. This is truly a vivid farce of a relative visit turning into a quarrel.

National Photography Exhibition to Be Held in Beijing and Shanghai 133

The International News Photography Society, to promote art and culture, plans to hold a national and international photography exhibition. This has been reported in various newspapers. It is now learned that the society has hired famous photographers from various regions, including Lang Jingshan, Zhang Yinquan, Wei Shouzhong, Zhao Cheng, Liu Xucang, Lu Shifu, Shu Shaonan, Chen Chuanlin, Wu Qianli, Chen Wanli, Ye Qianyu, Zhong Shanyin, and Xiang Huian, as organizing committee members for the National Photography Exhibition. Exhibitions will first be held in Beijing and Shanghai, and then they will be moved to various provinces in rotation. The international exhibition will be held after the opening of the domestic exhibition. Letters have been sent to various places to collect works. The nature of the works is generally defined as follows:

* Art Photography

* News Photography

* Scenic and Historic Sites

* Great Projects

* Local Customs

* Rural Factories

* Local Products

* Aviation and Air Defense Photography

* Medical Photography

* Underwater Photography

* Astronomical Photography

* Natural Science Specimen Photography

The format is uniformly 14 inches, horizontal or vertical is not limited, and cardboard is not required. The number of works per individual is limited to a maximum of ten, and the number of works per group is limited to a maximum of one hundred. The exhibition period is in mid-April. After the exhibition, it is planned to publish two special collections:

1. China's 25th Year Photography Yearbook

2. International Photography Exhibition Special Collection

The plan has been drafted, and the first preparatory meeting will be held in Shanghai in the coming days. The preparatory office is located at No. 26, Shibanqiao, Nanjing, and the collection office, in addition to the Beijing preparatory office, is also located at No. 14, Lane 37, Beihai Road, Shanghai. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Two-Railway Liaison Station Opens for Sale of Round-Trip Tourist Tickets Starting March 1st 134

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways and all joint transport stations are fully open for the sale of domestic joint transport round-trip tourist tickets, effective from March 1st of this year. This was announced yesterday by the two railway transportation departments in letters to the China Travel Service, American Express Bank, and the stations on the joint transport routes. According to document No. 7 from the Jinpu Railway Transportation Department's Passenger Transport Office regarding the newly revised procedures for the sale of joint transport round-trip tourist tickets, which had already been announced in documents Nos. 1 and 2, it is now stipulated that all joint transport stations on these two railways will also be fully open as points of sale for round-trip joint transport tourist tickets starting from March 1st of this year. The tourist destinations are the stations listed in the Attached Table of Stations for the Sale of Joint Transport Round-Trip Tourist Tickets in Annex to the 7th Edition of the Passenger Transport Regulations. The sales period is the period listed in the table, and the validity period is the period stipulated in the table, namely one month for distances within 1,000 kilometers and six weeks for distances beyond 1,000 kilometers. If the validity period printed on the ticket conflicts with the above regulations, the stations may correct it with a red ink pen and affix the stationmaster's seal for verification. In addition to requesting that the Accounting Department print and issue this joint transport round-trip tourist ticket, the letter is hereby issued to instruct the joint transport stations to comply. The round-trip fares and mileage tables from each joint transport station to each tourist destination are currently being compiled by the Railway Joint Transport Office and will be issued soon. Please inform the relevant personnel accordingly.

Commodity Inspection Bureau to Establish Livestock Quarantine Station: Infected Livestock Will Be Sent for Isolation; Site Has Been Selected, Construction to Begin This Week 136

Since the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau began conducting livestock inspections, all livestock with infectious diseases have been sent to the Veterinary Disease Prevention and Control Institute. It is now known that the bureau has decided to establish a livestock quarantine station in the central urban area and will invite bids for construction within this week. Details are as follows:

Site Selected, Construction to Begin Immediately: To establish the livestock quarantine station, the bureau has purchased ten acres of land near Zhaba Road and Shuidao Road in the central urban area. It has been decided to invite bids for construction within days, and the project is expected to be completed in May this year. After the completion of the station, the livestock inspection team of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau will send imported and exported livestock found to have infectious diseases to the station for isolation to prevent transmission, instead of sending them to the Jiangwan Veterinary Disease Prevention and Control Institute.

A Glimpse of the Quarantine Station's Facilities: Establishing a livestock quarantine station is a pioneering initiative in the country. The architectural design of the station has been finalized and includes five main buildings: livestock sheds, dissection room, incinerator, isolation ward, and office. Livestock with suspected infectious diseases will be sent to the isolation ward upon arrival, and several veterinarians will be hired to specialize in treatment. If livestock die of disease, they will be incinerated in the incinerator to prevent transmission.

Criminal Litigation Not Extinguished by Plaintiff's Death: Woman's Case Against Husband and Father-in-Law for Abandonment Unresolved, Plaintiff Now Deceased 138

Chen Cao Yanxiang, a woman residing at No. 3 Renqing Lane, Kunming Road, recently hired a lawyer with her four-year-old daughter Chen Xuechun to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court, accusing her husband Chen Wenzuo (residing at No. 770 Chengxue Lane, Tangshan Road) and her father-in-law Chen Yaosheng (residing at Huadong Tobacco Company, Tangshan Road) of abandonment. The court approved the case. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng convened a hearing in the Eighth Criminal Court. Neither of the defendants appeared in court; only the plaintiff's lawyer appeared, stating that the case had been settled and that Chen Cao Yanxiang had died of lung disease on the 13th of this month, requesting that the lawsuit be withdrawn. Judge Huang stated that this case was not a crime requiring a private prosecution and could not be withdrawn according to the law. Therefore, the defendants must appear in court for trial according to the law. If the plaintiff Chen Cao Yanxiang had indeed died, then according to the provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law, the court would notify the prosecutor to take over the litigation. The hearing was adjourned to a later date.

Old Woman Tragically Dies Under Bed on Qingyun Road 139

Neck Has Rope Marks and Knife and Axe Wounds

Son Fled, Major Suspect

Chen Weizhong, a local resident of No. 9 Qingyun Road, Zhabei, was 62 years old and made a living by collecting rent in Ankang Lane,. Shanxi Road Chen's first wife had passed away, and he married a widow, Sheng, as his second wife ten years ago. At that time, Chen's first wife had given birth to a son named Yueyun, who is now 31 years old and has married and had a grandson named Yizhuang, who is now ten years old and attending a nearby elementary school. When Sheng married into the family, she brought two sons, both grown up, one named Maode, who works at the Fourth Section Fire Brigade, and one named Maokun, who is unemployed at home. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, after Chen Weizhong went out to collect rent, only Sheng and her son Maokun were left at home. Around 12:00 PM, Chen returned home and found his old wife had been killed under the bed in the downstairs side room, with rope marks on her neck and knife and axe wounds, covered in blood, a horrific sight. He called for family members, but no one responded, as Yueyun, Maode, and others had gone out to work, and Maokun was also nowhere to be found. Chen ran to report to the Xibinxing Road Police Station under whose jurisdiction the matter fell, which in turn reported to the North Station Branch. They went to the scene together and confirmed the facts. The room was also sprinkled with kerosene, emitting an unusual odor, suggesting that the murderer intended to kill her and then set fire to the body to destroy the evidence. In addition to reporting the information to the Supervisory Office of the Public Security Bureau, the branch ordered the local guarantor to report to the Shanghai Local Court for an inquest. Around 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Liu Shiqing, Clerk Jiang Shaoji, and others arrived at the scene. The inquest determined that the deceased, Chen Sheng, had indeed been killed by others before her death. In addition to issuing a certificate for burial, the husband of the deceased was instructed to prepare a coffin for burial first, and then wait for the arrest of the murderer for further investigation. It is also heard that the deceased's son, Maokun, is currently on the run, so he is a major suspect.

The 270th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on February 15, 25th year of the Republic [1936]. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: A. The total amount of convertible notes issued is 23,155,9583 silver dollars, including 22,641,530 banknotes. The total amount of exchange note reserve is 23,155,9583 silver dollars, including a cash reserve of 16,749,7703 yuan. The cash reserve is deposited in the bank's issuing branches and sub-branches in the amount of 11,113,4583.51 yuan, and deposited with fellow banks in the amount of 5,636,319.49 yuan. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 64,061,880 silver dollars. B. The total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of the customs gold exchange note reserve is 271,324.70 yuan. The reserve includes 7351.25 taels of gold, which, at a price of 507, is equivalent to 371,324.70 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 21 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be guaranteed by legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%. The regulations are in compliance. This report is submitted. February 17, 25th year of the Republic of China. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fu, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Jun Qing, Qia Qing, Hou, Xu Ji."

Shanghai's Paper Industry 154

— Edited by China Huixin

(Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview - Part 14)

I. History 155

The papermaking industry, since the Han Dynasty, has been one of the most important industries in our country. Jiangxi, Hunan, Sichuan, Zhejiang, Guangdong, and other provinces are all famous paper-producing areas, with Jiangxi province producing the most. The Lian Shi paper and Mao Bian paper of Jiangxi and Fujian, the Xuan paper of Anhui (mainly produced in Xuancheng), and the Pi paper of Yunnan and Guizhou are all quite famous. However, the manufacturing methods are simple, and the scale is not large, all being old-fashioned handicraft production. The output is small, and the paper is expensive, which is not suitable for cooling down. ( ) Since the social and cultural undertakings ( ). With .

In the thirty-second year, due to poor business conditions, there were only renovations of old factories and no establishment of new factories. After the European War, the situation changed slightly, and many paper mills sprang up in Shanghai. In the fourteenth year of the Republic, the Jiangnan Paper Company was organized. In the fifteenth year, Tianju was established. In the sixteenth year, Minsheng followed (reorganized into Minsheng Yuji in the nineteenth year of the Republic). Yuantai and Huanshan both established branches in the eighteenth year of the Republic. The Shanghai Paper Mill was established in the twenty-first year of the Republic, and the Meijin and Dachina factories were established in the twenty-third year of the Republic. The above-mentioned are only those established in this port. As for other ports, new-style paper mills also appeared at the same time, such as the Wu, Hua, and He factories established in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces after the European War. Currently, there are more , which are all examples. From the Shen Bao of the twenty-fourth year of the Republic, it is recorded that there are a total of paper mills (including paper mills and paper users) in Shanghai, with only more than 300,000 yuan of capital and an annual output value of only more than 600,000 yuan. It is difficult to compete with foreign paper on all fronts. Therefore, there is still the unhealthy phenomenon of foreign paper flooding the domestic market, which needs to be rescued by the Chinese people.

II. Import of Foreign Paper 156

Foreign paper is a unified name, but there are actually distinctions between ordinary paper, cigarette paper, drawing paper, etc. At the same time, there are many countries importing, such as Sweden, Canada, Japan, the United States, etc., only those with larger amounts. According to statistics from the customs authorities, the import of foreign paper, according to its main categories, is listed as follows to get a glimpse: (Unit: Customs Gold)

Note: Ordinary paper is used for printing books and newspapers. The following table shows the position of each country in the foreign paper trade with China:

Comparison Table of Foreign Paper Imported to China by Country in the Twenty-fourth Year of the Republic of China (Unit: Customs )

Comparison Table of Foreign Paper Imported to China by Country in the Twenty-fourth Year of the Republic of China

From the previous table, we can see that the largest importer of foreign paper is the United States, followed by Japan, and then Canada and Germany. What is particularly noteworthy is the sharp increase in the amount of Japanese paper imported to our country. According to the statistics of the Paper Manufacturers Association, the import of Japanese paper to central China, the Northeast, Hong Kong, and other places in the first half of last year alone totaled 80,386,000 pounds, an increase of more than 10 million pounds compared to the same period last year. The influx of foreign goods has depressed domestic sales, which is what the Chinese people are paying attention to.

As for the imported Chinese paper, the main place for promotion is Shanghai, which is the center of national industry and commerce and the center of the foreign paper market. For example, in the twenty-third year, the imported general paper (total) was 7,530,532 , of which 4,517,681 passed through Shanghai, accounting for about 45% of the total import amount. As for the market situation of foreign paper in this port, it will be discussed later. (To be continued)

Shanghai New Life Movement Second Anniversary Special Issue

Edited by the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association

The Practice of the New Life Movement 157

— Wu Tiecheng

The New Life Movement, since its advocacy by Chairman Chiang, has now been two years. It deeply meets the needs of the times and is especially an important plan for the revival of the nation. Therefore, it can form a trend and be followed by the whole country.

Looking back at the history of China in recent times, various movements have emerged one after another. However, their effect is either only seen in the advocacy of a few people with lofty ideals, and not followed by the general public; or there is only temporary excitement, and no lasting power. Only the New Life Movement is different from this! The New Life Movement is the driving force for promoting new policies, reviving the nation, and advancing all cultural construction in China. The basic points of the New Life Movement lie in the spirit of "Renew yourself day after day, and keep renewing yourself," and in the determination of "All things before are like yesterday's death, and all things from now on are like today's birth," to eliminate all the bad habits and decadent trends that are stagnant at the bottom of society; to eradicate all the decadent habits that are deeply rooted in people's hearts; and to cultivate a new lifestyle habit of being steadfast, upright, uncompromising, and striving upward; so that the lives of the people of the whole country can be increasingly rationalized, scientized, productivized, revolutionized, militarized, modernized, and artisticized.

Life is the general term for all activities of human life, the various behaviors of propagating life. If the whole country, from top to bottom, officials are hypocritical and corrupt, the people are scattered and numb, adults are corrupt and mediocre, young people are degenerate and dissolute; the rich are cumbersome and extravagant; the poor are humble and chaotic, then to try to rectify the discipline of the country, maintain social order, and liberate and revive the entire nation-state, would it not be a reversal of fortune? Therefore, transforming life is not only an important plan to save the decadent trends and revitalize people's hearts, but also the driving force to revive the nation, promote new policies, and build all culture.

Chairman Chiang, the Initiator of the New Movement 158

Examining the past various movements of saving the country and transforming it, the reason why it is difficult to achieve results in the end, the key lies in being impractical and not considering the root. The relationship between the implementation of any system and social customs and people's habits is very close. China's past education, and even all politics, suffered from hypocrisy and did not seek practicality, resulting in ineffective laws, useless technology, and incompetent machines. The officials are the same, but the efficiency is different; the technology is the same, but the achievements are different; the machines are the same, but the functions are different. Therefore, any country, after reforming the old and establishing the new, must move it with wind and transform it with education, and then its politics can be governed. The work of changing customs and habits is more urgent than politics and education. The New Life Movement is admired by all nations, but today it still presents the image of the four virtues not being promoted and the discipline being abandoned. Even other countries openly use words like "unorganized" and "uncultured" as material for ridicule and abuse. This is not due to the ignorance of the Chinese nation, but due to the empty words and false pride of later generations, who cannot put it into practice.

Therefore, the essence of the boxing life movement lies in acting vigorously, not in empty words; the key to the success of the New Life Movement lies in the practice of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and not in propaganda in various forms.

Wang Yangming, a great Confucian of his generation, deeply knew the root of the diseases of our people, and therefore created the theory of the unity of knowledge and action. He said:

"Where knowledge is truly and firmly known, it is action; where action is clearly and keenly observed, it is knowledge;"

"There has never been knowledge without action; knowledge without action is merely not knowing;"

"The learning of sages is only one effort, knowledge and action cannot be divided into two things;"

"Knowledge is the beginning of action, and action is the completion of knowledge!"

Yan Yuan (Fei ), Li (Nu Gu) lived at the end of the Ming Dynasty; they both advocated the theory of vigorous action, in . Yan said:

"The people's learning, in the heart , the mouth talks. There are thousands of words , I don't know if the body does one thing as reality."

"Examine the reality of one end and one section, do not the whole body great use of ;"

"Cover only to practice kung fu, can not to language words on effort; the battle, famous Analects of Confucius; people recorded, is act."

" No , only in the word act , such as people's , but to force ."

That is to say, it is the central work of changing customs and habits, initiating people's hearts, and promoting the national destiny; it is also the basic movement that is extremely indispensable for the revival of the nation at present.

However, the promotion of this kind of movement depends on the self-consciousness and self-reliance of the people of the whole country, setting an example, so that they can promote themselves to others, popularize the whole country, form a trend of the times, and form the strength of the times. Our country was originally a country of etiquette and righteousness, and the teachings of the former sages and philosophers have long been .

His disciple Li , inherited his ambition; also said:

"The scriptures are the books for preparing the arts, so they are to teach practice, not to be read in vain." Today, on the second anniversary of the New Life Movement; I am honored to be asked to contribute a draft by the Association; I am ashamed to be unworthy, and I am a guide. I deeply worry that this basic movement to save the country and revive it will still follow the same path of empty words as in the past; because of its words, I would like to share my efforts. How will the achievements of the New Life Movement be in the future, and how will the fate of the Chinese nation be in the future, it only depends on how vigorously the people of the country will act in the future!

The New Life Movement and Saving the Country 159

— Wu Kaixian

The New Life Movement has been advocating for two years. In these two years, China's national crisis has become deeper and deeper. Today, our Chinese nation has really stepped onto the crossroads of survival and death. We can no longer dawdle and procrastinate. Today, as we commemorate the second anniversary of the New Life Movement, we must think about how the New Life Movement is related to saving the country and reviving the nation.

There are many people who look down on the New Life Movement. They think, "There is no magic formula for saving the country in it, and there will be no miracle of reviving the nation." Really? If it is really like this, then the New Life Movement is only a cause for times of peace, and it is really unnecessary now. Quite the opposite. The reason why we want to advocate the New Life Movement is because it has a great relationship with saving the country and reviving the nation.

Let's take a look at the social atmosphere now. What is the attitude of the general public towards life? Cowardice, selfishness, numbness, indifference, dissipation, decadence, laziness, contentment, fondness for petty cleverness, and using public office for private gain are all signs of national subjugation and decline. Previously, a Japanese ethnologist summarized the various bad qualities of the Chinese nation based on many old Chinese novels, saying that the Chinese nation was originally an inferior nation. Of course, he had his purpose in saying that, which made us very angry and unconvinced. However, when we think calmly, the descriptions in the novels are not sufficient to rely on; and there are indeed many things wrong with our people's customs and social atmosphere. We can still be very angry, we can only feel ashamed.

Now, our nation is about to step on the line of death. We must seek survival in death, strive for regeneration, and bear the heavy burden of relieving the national crisis and reviving the nation. This heavy burden cannot be shouldered by cowards, selfish people, numb people, or indifferent people. It cannot be shouldered by people who are dissipated, decadent, lazy, or content. It cannot be shouldered by people who use public office for private gain or who are fond of petty cleverness. Quite the opposite, these people are destined to be slaves to a conquered country and traitors. This kind of attitude towards life and social atmosphere is a great enemy to the future of relieving the national crisis and reviving the nation.

The New Life Movement is to fundamentally eliminate this atmosphere of national subjugation that permeates the entire nation. It is to make every Chinese person change their appearance, wash their hearts, and be reborn, to extricate themselves from the decadent view of life. Therefore, the new life that we seek is definitely not just the "basic common sense life of a civilized person" that some people have left; but has:

A view of life dedicated to the national revolution and dedicated to the revival of the nation.

A kind of pure, loyal, selfless spirit.

A kind of good character of knowing etiquette, righteousness, integrity, shame, responsibility, and discipline.

Etc., and living an orderly, clean, simple, frugal, hard-working life. Only people who live such a life can bear the responsibility of relieving the national crisis and reviving the nation; and only such a life is the new life we seek during our national crisis.

We examine the progress of the New Life Movement in the past two years and know that our journey is still very long; but our nation and environment urgently need us to make even greater efforts! Comrades! Strive!

The New Life Movement in Extraordinary Times 160

— Pan Gong

What is universally recognized in 1926?

Modern is complicated, not pure, now the world is a whole organic organization, not indifferent. Because the development of transportation has shortened the world's journey, and the progress of industry and commerce has increased the close chain of mankind, the war between one country and another often affects the interests of other countries, and is involved in the war. The past World War I and the recent Italian-Ethiopian War, in which Britain came forward to intervene, are all obvious examples for us. Therefore, although we are determined to be peaceful and do not want war, under certain circumstances, it is not allowed by affection. The world's situation is so urgent, and our country's environment is very dangerous. Imperialist wars are forced to go to war for colonies, or to go to war for survival, or to go to war for national salvation. Since it is a war of life and death, how should we deal with it prudently, so as to avoid the tragedy of the destruction of the country and the nation! Some people say: This is the responsibility that the government should bear. The purchase of military supplies, the design of transportation, the storage of food, and the liaison of diplomacy are all things that the government should do, and not things that the people can do. It is true that the various things mentioned above are the preparations that the government should have, but with only the above preparations, is there a guarantee of victory? Modern warfare does not only rely on the fighting on the battlefield, but the mutual struggle of the entire nation. The quality of the people is the standard for the victory or defeat of the war. What the government does is only planning and command, but the real strength is completely in each of our people. If we can really unify our thinking, be orderly in our steps, be uncompromising in the face of adversity, and be able to endure hardship, then 400 million people will be as one, and the strength of 400 million people can create a great force. With this great force, to deal with the current extraordinary situation, we will definitely be able to overcome ourselves by force. But how to cultivate this great power? Two years ago, Chairman Chiang advocated the New Life Movement in Nanchang, which had already revealed to us that if we can earnestly operate it, this is the only effective way to save the country. The New Life Movement is to promote "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and since the Opium War, our country has signed countless treaties that have humiliated the country, and the general public is still unaware. In the past four years, the explicit and implicit plunder of the imperialists has made people feel heartbroken! We talk about saving the country, but in reality we are still extravagant and lazy, which is against the word "shame" in the New Life Movement. In other words, we don't know "shame". Therefore, if we want to know "shame", we should practice a new life. Now all countries are striving to improve the race in order to cultivate excellent citizens, so in the innate aspect, they are all advocating eugenics, and in the acquired aspect, they are focusing on education. However, the critical situation in our country is imminent, and there is no time to wait, so we advocate the New Life Movement to assist the lack of education. Therefore, the New Life Movement is also a movement to improve the quality of the people."

However, the improvement of the quality of the people is by no means a work that can be accomplished overnight. At the same time, the so-called quality of the people does not refer to one aspect, but includes knowledge, skills, morality, and physical fitness. In this extraordinary period, the most important goal at present that needs to be practiced is "observing discipline" and "enduring hardship". Without discipline, there will be no strength; without enduring hardship, nothing can be accomplished. When two countries are at war, the frontline soldiers must obey military orders, endure hardship, and even the people in the rear must absolutely abide by the laws, and give the invading country an opportunity. In the outline of the New Life Movement, it says, "The New Life Movement is a revolution in the lives of all our people. With the simplest and most urgent methods, we eliminate the habits of our people that are incompatible with the times and the environment, and make them tend to a life that is suitable for the times and the environment. In other words, we seek to rationalize the lives of the people." Therefore, the new life, that is, a rational life, is a life that adapts to the times and the environment. Mr. Sun Yat-sen once said that the Chinese people are a heap of loose sand. If we want the loose sand to be united, then we must all abide by discipline. China is a country with backward production and is in a semi-colonial position. If we want to save consumption and save the country, we must be able to endure hardship.

The promotion of the New Life has been going on for two years now. Although some effects have been achieved in these two years, on the whole , it has not been able to change the atmosphere of society, and most of the people have not abandoned the habits of extravagance and laziness, especially in terms of , they are still floating and young , with little .

Xiqing Decides to Resume this Year's Women's Basketball Tournament —Using Women's Rules— 164

Letters were sent to various teams inviting them to participate. Registration will begin immediately. Each team must pay a registration fee of five yuan and purchase twenty yuan worth of tickets.

The Western Young Men's Christian Association of Jing'an Temple Road in this city has always been very active in promoting sports. After the conclusion of this year's men's basketball league, it originally planned to continue to hold the women's basketball league. Later, due to the use of men's rules, few people participated. The association then decided to stop the event and immediately began to prepare for the 8th volleyball league, which opened last night. Because the Detelphon Yiling team and others initiated a resumption, and discussed the matter with Chinese and Western teams, the Women's Basketball Association sent a letter to the Xiqing Sports Committee requesting a reconsideration. Yesterday, Li Yuxian of the Xiqing Sports Department told reporters that the association has decided to resume holding this year's women's basketball league and will adopt women's rules. Each participating team must pay a registration fee of five yuan and a deposit of twenty yuan for the purchase of tickets. Letters have been sent to Chinese and Western teams inviting them to participate. Registration has now begun. It is hoped that all teams will join as soon as possible so that the competition can be launched as soon as possible.

Shanghai Basketball Association 165

Zhenru Defeats Donghua

Liangxi Beats Aurora

The Shanghai Basketball Association held another Jiajia Group match yesterday between Zhenru and Donghua. In the first ten minutes, the teams were evenly matched. After that, Zhenru was able to play freely, and as a result, defeated Donghua 56 to 35. In the other B group match, Liangxi defeated Aurora 60 to 27.

Both the Zhenru and Donghua teams had players selected to attend the Yalin Pace representative. The other generals were also talented at the time, and their strengths were equal, so they were all cautious. Seeing Feng Nianhua's agility, Wang Nanzhen, who had been a forward, was reappointed as a defender to monitor Little Feng and allow Cai Yanxiong to take advantage of the situation. Zhenru's deployment was very effective.

Donghua used its usual lineup. It was difficult for Feng Nianhua to develop, and Lu Zhongen's defense was more than enough, but his offense was insufficient. Only Chen Xianglong was able to do anything. Because of his lack of experience, Lu Zhongyu often let the enemy disrupt the defense, so apart from creating an 8-8 tie in the first ten minutes, there was little opportunity to raise his head.

Before the game started, Yan Yunjin committed a foul, and Feng Nianhua scored three points. Zhenru's Cai, Kuang, and Yan attacked the basket four times, taking an 8-3 lead. Soon, Donghua's Sun and Chen scored points, creating an 8-8 tie. The spring colors were evenly divided. After that, the Zhenru players launched a major offensive, taking the lead. From then on, they continued to increase the score. Struggling until halftime, Zhenru was 33 and Donghua was 15.

After a short break, the competition resumed. Chen Xianglong took the opportunity to attack, scoring twice. Kuang Yao Ya returned the favor, without distinction. Then Chen Xianglong scored three three-pointers, and Sun Baoqing scored in the middle. This was closer, reaching 28 to 39. Then, Cai and Han frequently invaded Donghua. Sun and Chen defended left and right, but they were unable to prevent the attacks. As a result, the situation declined sharply. Holding on until time ran out, Zhenru won 56 to 35.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Revises Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools: Operational Goals Emphasize National Consciousness, Reduce Total Teaching Time; Secondary Schools Consider Students' Individuality, Primary Schools Adapt to Practical Needs—Primary Schools to Merge Subjects, Textbooks to Change— 168

Junior and Senior High Schools (Nanjing, 18th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education announced revisions to the teaching subjects and hours for junior and senior high schools on the 18th. The main points are as follows: Emphasis on cultivating students' initiative in learning and reducing their course load. The total number of teaching hours per week in junior high school has been reduced from 34-35 hours to 31 hours, and in senior high school, it has been reduced from 31-34 hours to approximately 29 hours. Emphasis on national consciousness, enriching the curriculum standards for various subjects in junior and senior high schools, and adding teaching materials on national spirit to subjects such as Civics, Chinese, History, and Geography. Consideration of students' individuality, stipulating that from the second year of senior high school, students can be divided into Group A and Group B. Students who are inclined towards natural sciences can study more mathematics, while those who are inclined towards literature, history, and social sciences can study less mathematics and more subjects such as Chinese, Logic, and English as alternatives. Consideration for students who do not continue their education, stipulating that senior high schools may, depending on local conditions, offer simplified vocational subjects (such as commercial accounting, bookkeeping, statistics, applied writing, typing, agronomy, horticulture, cooperatives, etc.) as elective subjects in the final year, so that those who cannot continue their education can still prepare for employment. In addition, the Ministry of Education is also working on compiling editorial outlines for each subject to facilitate teaching.

Kindergartens and Primary Schools (Nanjing, 18th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education announced revisions to the curriculum standards for kindergartens and primary schools on the 18th. The main points are as follows: Reduction of the total teaching time at all levels. The total teaching time is 1020 minutes for the first grade, 1110 minutes for the second grade, 1230 minutes for the third grade, 1290 minutes for the fourth grade, and 1380 minutes for the fifth and sixth grades. Compared with the original total time, the average reduction at each level is more than one-tenth. Merging of subjects and parts of the knowledge of social studies, nature, and hygiene in the middle grades. Hygiene habits are incorporated into civic training and merged into the "Common Knowledge" subject. Manual labor and art in the lower grades are merged into the "Work" subject. Physical education and music are merged into the "Singing and Games" subject. Part of the knowledge of hygiene in the higher grades is merged into the "Nature" subject. Revising the operational requirements of the curriculum standards. There are two goals for the revision: 1. Special emphasis on national consciousness; 2. Adapting to practical needs. Furthermore, the Ministry of Education has also hired experts to draft the revision of the entire curriculum and the new curriculum standards for each subject, which will be announced soon. In view of the revision of the curriculum standards, there will be inevitable changes in primary school textbooks. It is heard that the Ministry of Education plans to convene responsible personnel from various publishing houses in the near future to discuss this issue.

Funds for Public Education Societies in Various Counties of Jiangsu to Be Included in Central People's Schools: Awaiting the Promulgation of Regulations Before Distributing - Jiangsu Education and Finance Departments Issue Instructions to Comply 170

Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education and the Department of Finance received a report from the Tongshan County Government regarding how to budget for the expenses of compulsory education classes and the People's and Agricultural Education Centers in the 25th year. The following instructions were issued: "The report has been received. It has been investigated that the provincial subsidy for each county's additional compulsory education classes for the entire 12 months should be included in the revenue and expenditure budget for the 25th year. Together with the number of compulsory education classes handled with the contingency funds from the local general budget used in the 24th year, it will serve as the standard for the total amount of increased education and cultural expenses allocated to each county in the 25th year. The compulsory education class expenses of the county should naturally be included in the education budget, in the section for compulsory education, People's and Agricultural Education Centers (Baoshan, Danyang, Funing, Lianshui, Suqian, Yixing, Ganyu, Qidong - Eight County Experimental Agricultural Education Centers, and educational halls in Nantong and other counties implementing the integration of politics and education), extracurricular activities in the People's Education Experimental Zone, and the original expenses of public stadiums. These should all be included under the item of Central People's Schools. Await the promulgation of regulations before distributing in detail. You are to relay these instructions for compliance."

Mayor Wu Visits Aurora University 175

Mayor Wu Tiecheng visited Aurora University on Luban Road yesterday afternoon. After lunch, all teachers and students held a meeting in the university's auditorium to welcome him. First, the mayor gave a speech, stating that schools are the foundation of national organization, and students who receive university education are a very small number of the entire population. They should be deeply aware of the advantages of their circumstances and the importance of their responsibilities. The purpose of education is to seek the way of being human, and they should accept education with the utmost sincerity. With this sincerity, they will know to reflect on themselves, improve their character, and work hard in their studies, so that they can complete their studies and not disgrace their ancestors, but increase their abilities for the country and society. Then, Principal Hu Yi reported on the recent situation of the school. The meeting adjourned at 3:30 PM.

Da Zhong Emphasizes Scout Training 177

Da Zhong Middle School on Kunshan Road in this city has a long history. Its graduates are all over the country. In past graduation exams, the results have been excellent, and it has received a first-class certificate from the Education Bureau. Since Mr. Wu Ruinian, a Master of Chemistry from Columbia University in the United States, took over last autumn, he has strived to improve the school, and the school's affairs have progressed and prospered. The students' level has improved, and the academic atmosphere is simple and honest, which is deeply trusted by students and parents. This spring, new students are very enthusiastic. It is heard that Principal Wu, in view of the increasingly urgent national crisis, in addition to strictly training military knowledge, is making great efforts to emphasize scout training in junior high school. Chen, the full-time scout instructor of the school, has formulated a program for implementation, and is expanding various facilities and hiring Mr. Zhou Zhongpei, who once served as the band instructor of the provincial Shanghai Middle School, as the band instructor.

From the New Life Movement to the Great Learning 180

— Zhang Shouyong

Mr. Chiang has been promoting the New Life Movement for two years, and recently he spoke about the Great Learning. Shouyong is a bookworm who is still making a living in old papers at the age of sixty-one. Recalling two years ago, he wrote an article on the basic concepts of the New Life Movement in Yunhua Bimonthly, recognizing the New Life Movement as a new life for humanity. Everyone thinks about protecting this new life, and everything that can harm our life is regarded as a pest. Success can be achieved, and fame can be established. I advise everyone to divide the restoration of rites, exemplifying righteousness, cultivating integrity, and knowing shame into four major parts to govern the inner self, and to use the outline, central theory, public purpose, etc. as the standards for implementation. I also advise everyone to pay extra attention to practice. Later, I heard Mr. Chiang advocate the Three Transformations in the New Life Movement, namely militarization, artification, and industrialization, and I felt that these three transformations were truly the only way to save the country and the people. Recently, I heard Mr. Chiang talk about the Great Learning, with tens of thousands of words, deeply penetrating people's minds. Shouyong once said that there are gains and losses in things, but there is no ancient or modern in the Way. Confucius said, "Reviewing the old and knowing the new." Zhu Xi said, "The old is what has been heard before, and the new is what is gained now." Mr. Chiang applies the ancient people's way of governing the country and pacifying the world to today, to the trend of the world, and expounds it without leaving anything out. He does not advocate hegemonic achievements but speaks of the kingly way. The kingly way lies in renewing the people. The three major principles of the Great Learning are to manifest illustrious virtue, to renovate the people, and to rest in the highest excellence. It also says, "Although Zhou was an old state, its mandate was renewed." Zhu Xi said, "New means to get rid of the old." "If you can one day renovate yourself, let there be a daily renovation. Yea, let there be continuous renovation." Eliminate all kinds of old habits, and then a new life can be established. Therefore, the New Life Movement and the Great Learning are connected everywhere. The Great Learning says, "As a mother cares for her infant." If one sincerely seeks it, though one may not hit the mark, one will not be far from it. Caring for an infant is the most ordinary thing, why is it used as a metaphor? Because an infant is also seeking life. If life is stabilized, the infant will not cry. Everyone can do the New Life Movement, then everyone can stop crying. Therefore, recognize that the New Life Movement is a new life. Now, if you want to escape from death, you can only go this way. Walking this way is the way of the Golden Rule of the Great Learning, that is, the way of manifesting illustrious virtue, renovating the people, and resting in the highest excellence. I hope everyone will appreciate Mr. Chiang's painstaking efforts in promoting it and walk this ever-renewing road, never to stray onto the wrong path and lose the vivacity.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (180) 181

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Meg felt that she had not done wrong to invite them to come when she heard it; because this child not only gave her a consolation, knowing that it was the voices of those children he loved most that were singing the last lullaby for John, but also in their faces, she saw the purity with which they had already felt the deepest emotion of virtue, and the impression given by the worthy being who was breathing his last before them would remain in their hearts for a long time and serve as a benefit. Little May's head was on her lap, Xiao Qiao was holding her hand, often watching her, his eyes quite like his father's, and some of his gestures seemed to be saying, "Don't worry, mother; I'm here"; and around her were reliable and lovable friends; so the patient, devout Meg let go of her heavy sorrow, and felt that her best help was to embrace the purpose of "life is for service" and do as her John had done.

That night, the moon was white and the wind was clear. The children of Plumfield were sitting on the steps as usual, and they naturally had to talk about the day's events.

Amy, who was always impatient, was the first to speak, "Uncle Fritz is the most understanding, Uncle Laurie is the happiest, but Uncle John is just the best; of all the people I've met, I only want to be like him."

"So do I. Didn't you hear what those people told old Papa today? I would be satisfied if someone could praise me like that after I died"; said Frank, regretting that he hadn't been able to appreciate Uncle John's goodness before.

"What did they say?" asked Jack, who was quite moved by the scenes he had seen today.

Tennessee Valley Authority Electrical Lawsuit Verdict, New York Stock Market Suffers Huge Shock

Initially Soared Ten Yuan, Then Fell Back Down 185

Newli Foreign Firm Report: Yesterday (17th), the New York stock market experienced huge fluctuations, and trading was as active as it had not been since July 10-11, 1933, with 9 million shares. When Chief Justice Hughes of the Supreme Court read out the verdict on the Tennessee Valley Authority electrical lawsuit, speculation wrongly predicted that the government would lose, and public utility stocks surged. The teleprinter market reached six minutes, and prices soared, with the largest increases reaching as much as ten yuan. Later, when it was heard that the government had won the lawsuit, the situation changed, and buyers contracted. The market appeared very chaotic, and speculators with insufficient reserves had to sell other stocks. Dozens of new highs also disappeared in a flash. However, low-priced automobile stocks and morning stocks continued to rise. Near the close, the situation stabilized slightly due to short covering. Small exchange stocks fell steadily, and the bond market was slightly lower. The full-day transaction volume was 4.72 million shares. The New York Index is listed on the left.

Vegetable Boat 205

— Xia Fei

Dongshan and Xishan in Dongting face each other. In the 36,000 acres of vast Taihu Lake, although the distance is only 18 miles, the only thing that maintains traffic between the two mountains is a vegetable boat. The vegetable boat is the one that carries vegetables from Dongshan to Xishan every day for sale, and also gives people a ride. It travels back and forth twice a day, departing from the front of Dongshan Mountain in the morning and arriving at Zhenxia Jiangli, and returning from Zhenxia to Dongshan in the evening. However, when it comes, it is carrying a boatload of vegetables and a few villagers—the people of Dongshan all call each other villagers—but when it goes back, there are many empty baskets and a few vegetable sellers left.

Debin, the owner of that broken little boat at 9 o'clock, and his wife have spent more than 20 years relying on the vegetable boat. Although they are always exposed to the sun in Taihu Lake in summer, and drink the northwest wind in Taihu Lake in winter, regardless of wind, rain, cold or warmth, they tightly bind their two lives to that little boat to struggle in Taihu Lake, but life is still okay; and they bought a few acres of land and built three houses.

The fare for taking the vegetable boat is sixteen copper coins per person, and it is also sixteen copper coins for loading one dan of vegetables; on average, there are fifteen people and ten dan of vegetables on their boat, plus the return trip, so they can earn more than two yuan a day. But apart from the couple, their son is also very frugal.

A Gentleman Has Awe 206

—

Logically, they have more than two yuan of income every day, and the expenses will not reach one yuan, and they should have saved a lot of money. But it is said that although they built three houses and bought a few acres of land on the surface, they actually owed a lot of debt to others; the reason is very simple, because Debin likes to drink and gamble, and women like to eat and dress, so although they勉强积得点, it is actually extremely limited.

Recently, there has been a small gasoline boat running between the east and west mountains of Dongting. Therefore, although the average villager felt a lot of convenience, Debin's vegetable boat still ran as usual, but business was very miserable!

Yan Zhenqing is a Native of Shandong 207

— Among Them

In the previous issue of this publication, Mr. Jiaoxin's article "Doubts About Notables from Various Provinces" stated that Yan Zhenqing was from Zhejiang, citing the "Tang Dynasty, Linyi native" entry in the Ciyuan dictionary as proof. I believe Mr. Jiaoxin is mistaken. As it concerns the native place of a distinguished predecessor, I am writing to correct it.

Upon investigation, there is no place called "Linyi" in Zhejiang. Linyi is in Shandong Province, and was called "Linyi" in ancient times. During the Qing Dynasty, it was renamed "Yizhou Prefecture," and it is now called "Linyi County." Those who have read the Analects of Confucius generally know the sentence: "Five or six adults wearing hats, six or seven children, bathing in the Yi River." Those who have studied geography also know that there is a river called the "Yi River" in Shandong, and Linyi is located beside this Yi River. (Of course, beside the Yi River there is also a county called "Yishui.") Linyi is located in southern Shandong, only about two hundred li from Donghai in Jiangsu Province. Most of the goods transported to Linyi are transferred from Haizhou in Jiangsu to boats on the Yi River. Because Linyi can transport foreign goods from Haizhou, it has become the commercial center of southern Shandong. There are two provincial middle schools there, one being "Linyi Middle School," and the other being a rural normal school. On the walls of the rural normal school, one can find traces of ancient inscriptions on broken stone fragments, some of which bear the calligraphy of Yan Zhenqing. According to the people of Linyi, it is Yan Zhenqing's hometown. Wang Xizhi also visited Linyi, but Wang Xizhi is not called a native of Linyi, Shandong. Furthermore, Yan Zhenqing is also called "Duke Lu of Yan," and "Lu" refers to Shandong. Therefore, I believe Mr. Jiaoxin is wrong to call Yan Zhenqing a native of Zhejiang.

West Lake in the Snow 208

— Zeng Jinke

Because I seemed to have grown tired of living in Shanghai, I went to Hangzhou. Is Hangzhou "Paradise"? Not necessarily. The concept of "Paradise" seems worth reconsidering now, doesn't it? However, I firmly believe that Hangzhou is a good place. The air in Hangzhou is different from the air in Shanghai. Naturally, the society in Hangzhou is also quieter than the society in Shanghai. People living in Shanghai always feel that they are living in a constant rush, constantly being made tense. In Hangzhou, everything feels very peaceful, and one can live very leisurely. Of course, West Lake and Hidden Tianzhu are also more lovable than the so-called "Bund of Ten Miles."

Several heavy snowfalls have adorned West Lake with even more beauty. "Searching for plum blossoms in the snow" is also a very poetic endeavor. So, my friend and I walked to Gushan (Solitary Hill). We didn't take a car because we wanted to leisurely appreciate the lake and mountains after the snowfall. This was my friend's excellent suggestion.

We walked slowly along the lake like we were taking a stroll. From the Sixth Workers' Corps to Broken Bridge, the "Remnant Snow on Broken Bridge" was already enough to admire. A new, very elegant little red building has been erected near the bridge, which is very cute. If a pair of poet spouses or two or three young and beautiful girls lived inside, the lake and mountains, if they had consciousness, would surely welcome their companions with great joy; it is a pity that such a good house, in such a good location, is actually an official "Tourist Bureau"! We walked to the lakeside of the Inner West Lake. The Su Causeway is like a jade belt tied around the waist of the West Lake. The myriad peaks, draped in white, were particularly touching. Looking around from the Bojuehui Bridge, the scenery was truly picturesque and breathtaking. The fragrance of the plum blossoms on Gushan had already reached the bridge to welcome us, so we had no choice but to abandon the snow scene and go to Gushan. Fanghe Pavilion was deserted, without a single tourist. The plum blossoms on Gushan were in full bloom, making me recall the famous lines "Sparse shadows slant across the clear, shallow water, faint fragrance drifts in the twilight moon." I imagine Lin Bu, Feng Xiaoqing, Su Xiaoxiao, and Su Manshu, all enjoying this beautiful scenery happily in the underworld, and congratulating themselves on being buried in this land? (At the same time, I thought of the two thousand white plum blossoms on Izusan in Atami, Japan.)

My friend was visiting for the first time. Every time we arrived at a scenic spot, he lingered, unwilling to leave. When we got to Gushan and saw so many plum blossoms, he was even more delighted. I originally wanted to pick two plum blossoms to take home and display in a vase on my desk, but my friend dissuaded me, so I didn't pick them. If everyone picked flowers, wouldn't later visitors have no flowers to see?

After descending Gushan, we lingered for a long time in front of the tomb of Yan Shu, the Venerable. The tragic fate of this talented poet is worthy of sympathy. Two years ago, at a banquet of the Southern Society, Mr. Liu Yazi gave me "The Complete Works of Yan Shu," from which I can imagine his literary talent and romantic charm. We then casually went to Yue Fei's Temple, where there were many tourists. I bought a copy of Yue Fei's handwritten "Man Jiang Hong" and "Chu Shi Biao," and also a print of the "Buddhist Scriptures Stored in the Leifeng Pagoda." It was already "dusk" when I got home.

Places Visited

Trip to Little Wang Mountain 209

— Shou Juan

I have long heard of the name Little Wang Mountain, and have repeatedly wanted to visit, but have had no opportunity, and only sighed in vain. On the Ren Day of the Bingzi year, I received an invitation from Mr. Li Yinzhai, the owner of the mountain, so I happily went. The day before, the famous Mr. Xu Ziqiu and his friend Mr. Li Jinzhang came to meet me, saying that we could first go to Mr. Li's residence in Liucun, stay overnight, and then plan a trip to Little Wang Mountain. I agreed, so I sent my son, and took a motorcar, changed to a sedan chair, and went with them. After twelve li, we arrived at Liucun. The place was extremely secluded, as if in another world. There was a mountain called Jade Screen Mountain, with jagged rocks, and bizarre lights and shadows, as if a jade screen was being unfolded. In the morning, we went to climb the mountain together. Because the mountain slope was steep, and the wind was particularly strong, we could not reach the summit, and hastily descended. After lunch, we set off for Little Wang Mountain, which was about five li away. When we arrived, the host had not yet arrived, so we drank tea and chatted while waiting. Soon, we heard the sound of dogs barking, and someone shouting, so we quickly went out to see. The host had arrived. Those who came with him were Madam Tang Guoli, the wife of Zhang Taiyan, and her sons Qi and Huizi Xinke; and our old friends Mr. Fan Yanqiao and Mr. Jin Shoumei also arrived later, all having just come from the city. After exchanging greetings, we chatted happily. After Mr. Yin Gong retired from his tired official life, he lived in seclusion in Wuzhong and never came out again, enjoying the mountains and rivers in the autumn osmanthus season. Later, he obtained Little Wang Mountain near Mount Qiong, and bought it. He buried his mother at the foot of the mountain, built a tomb and village, and then proceeded to manage the entire mountain, clearing weeds, planting fine trees, establishing schools, and building roads, diligently and tirelessly, until now. Compared to those who sell their souls in the pursuit of fame and fortune, how great is the difference between the worthy and the unworthy? After a short rest, we asked to tour the mountain. Mr. Yin Gong enthusiastically led the way. We climbed Xiaojingshou, where Mr. Taiyan wrote an inscription, made in the Great Seal script, which was carved on stone by a famous calligrapher, with an extremely ancient, simple, and elegant effect. Then we visited the Jifeng Cave, Chuiyu Guest, Cuiyun Peak, and Woshi Peak, and ascended Hushantang. Looking out, we could see only mountains, and our hearts and minds were broadened. So we took a group photo outside the hall to commemorate the occasion. The most unforgettable thing was the boundless pine forest, thousands upon thousands of trees, forming a magnificent sight, looking like a green sea. When the wind passed through, the sound was like the waves of the Xiang River. In the autumn of the Jiaxu year, the old poet Mr. Chen Shiyi came to visit, and praised it, saying: "This is a pine sea!" Mr. Yin Gong was pleased, and quickly asked Mr. Shi to write a wall inscription, which was carved on stone to record the event. There are many cliffs in the mountain, with inscriptions, poems, and couplets, all written by famous figures, which are extremely precious. Inscriptions such as Mr. Taiyan's "Little Longzhong," Qi Piaohu Guangsheng's "Stone Forest," Mr. Zhang Zhongren's "Mountain Colors, Lake Light, Pine Waves, and Snow Waves," and Mr. Li Xiehe's "Secluded and Beautiful Green," etc. Poems such as Mr. Zhang Daoyou's "Deep Green Forms a Sea, Mountain Walks Clear After Snow. The Year's End Wind is Strong, Come Here to Hear the Sound of Pines," Mr. Deng Xiaoke's "The Yin Side of the Mountain is Covered with Ten Thousand Pines, Lofty People and Wise Scholars Follow Each Other, How Majestic and Not Accepting the Title of Daifu," Mr. Zhang Puquan's "The Great King Divined a Residence on Little Wang Mountain, Wild Clothes and Sandals, Meaning Naturally Leisurely, Remotely Pointing at the Boundless Hatred of the Wu Palace, The Autumn Moon Over Lake Tai, a Single Sandbar," etc.; Couplets such as Mr. Yin Gong's self-written "Clouds Rise from Stone Mountains, Wind Enters the Pines Below and is Clear," Mr. Taiyan's "This Old Man Knows a Thousand and One Things, Mr. Shares the Concerns of Later Generations," etc.; it is impossible to record them all. After the tour, we went together to pay respects to Madam Taijun's tomb, bowing three times and retreating. After dinner, Yanqiao took out a booklet and wrote a travel poem, inviting all the fellow travelers to write inscriptions. Madam Zhang responded with a poem, saying: "Don't Refuse to Go Far to Explore the Scenery, Don't Complain About the Deep Mountains for Dwelling, In the Vast Pine Sea, There Should Be an Old Dragon Roaring." I also reluctantly responded with twenty characters, which are not worth saving. Then Mr. Yin Gong repeatedly urged us to write poems, saying they were for carving on the cliffs. Yanqiao and Madam Zhang each wrote a joint poem. Zhang Gongzi Qi, who was only twelve years old, wielded his brush and wrote the two characters "Qi An" in the ancient clerical script, with truly silver hooks and iron strokes; I humbly added the four characters "Zhen Song Shou Shi," which were merely scribbles. After the writing was completed, we joined Mr. Yin Gong and discussed world affairs, feeling overwhelmed with emotion. It was almost noon when we went to bed, and I seemed to still hear the angry waves of the pine sea in my dream. The next morning, when we were about to leave, Mr. Yin Gong insisted on keeping us, and we made a promise to meet again, and then parted.

Little Western Heaven 210

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Fourth: For Profit, a Beauty is Slighted; a Clumsy Fellow Reluctantly Parts; With High Ambitions and Strong Feet, a Robust Man Ventures into the Wilderness.

Jia Duocai pondered for a moment and said with a smile, "That's fine too. Let the two of you go back and ask first. I'll assume a number for now. Whoever offers a fair price, we here will definitely add another thousand yuan to it. For example, if someone offers twelve thousand, and can't add any more, we'll offer thirteen thousand." Bei Hai shook his head and smiled, "Mr. Jia's method is a bit inappropriate. If I collude with someone else and set the price very high, would Mr. Jia still be able to add a thousand yuan in the same way?" Jia Duocai picked up his hand again, rubbed it around his ear a few times, smiled, and shook his head slightly, saying, "I think that wouldn't be the case, would it? For example, if you really set the price very high, beyond what is reasonable, do you think I would still be able to add a thousand yuan? If the people from your Prince's Mansion really intend to sell this piece of land and free up some money to use, they would naturally be willing to make the deal, and wouldn't raise the land price to an unmanageable level." Bei Hai smiled faintly and said, "That's not necessarily the case. It is said that property is not sold to the chief strategist." Jia Duocai picked up his wine glass, drank two mouthfuls in a row, then poured a full glass, raised it, and looked like he was about to drink but hadn't yet, smiling slightly, "That's certainly true. But there are people with strange temperaments, who insist on selling their property to the chief strategist. Why is that? It's for the sake of earning a few more dollars." After he finished speaking, he suddenly made his smile even bigger, shook his hand at Bei Hai, and said, "I'm not advising you to sell your property to the chief strategist. I'm saying that my temperament is just like that. Mr. Wang, if I have something that you are plotting, I would be willing to sell it to you, do you believe it or not?" After he said this, he widened his eyes and looked at Bei Hai. Bei Hai couldn't say what kind of stimulus he was receiving, he only felt a heat on his face, and even his eyelids were a little unable to lift. Jia Duocai then stopped talking to him, turned to Wang Shicheng and said with a smile, "This Mr. Wang, don't be suspicious. If a deal doesn't go through, there's still goodwill. Even if this land deal falls apart, we are still friends. When doing things in society, we can't always look at money, and we can't always look at business. Mr. Wang, if you ever need my help in the future, I will definitely still help. Come, Mr. Wang, I'll fill your glass." As he spoke, he picked up the wine pot and poured it into Wang Shicheng's glass, laughing, "Just drink, if you get drunk, just go lie down in my room." (405)

After using them, the effects were remarkable. Not only were her menstruation and discharge regulated, and all symptoms disappeared, but her uterus was also warm and her body strong, restoring the youthful beauty of her maiden days. Her breasts and buttocks were high and full, fully displaying the inherent curves of a young woman.
